It is proposed to transfer Li Shijia, Director of the General Affairs Department, to fill the vacancy. The vacant position of Director of the General Affairs Department is proposed to be filled by Yang Qingzhen, Director of the Military Evaluation Department. Please review and approve the appointments and removals. Resolution: Approved. (7) Minister Chen of the Navy submitted a request to dismiss Zhu Tiansen, Colonel Counselor of the Ministry, due to reassignment. Resolution: Approved. (8) Minister He of the Ministry of Military Administration submitted a request to approve the resignation of Liu Guoming, Brigade Commander of the 95th Brigade of the 32nd Division, due to illness. It is proposed to promote Gao Guojun, Deputy Brigade Commander of the 94th Brigade of the same division, to fill the vacancy. Resolution: Approved. A list is prepared and requested for review and approval of the appointments and removals. Resolution: Approved. (12) Minister He of the Ministry of Military Administration submitted a request that Li Zubai, Colonel and Brigade Commander of the 239th Brigade of the 79th Division, and Zhang Ying, Major General and Brigade Commander of the 237th Brigade of the same division, should be dismissed due to reassignment. It is also requested to appoint Li Deshan as the Colonel Deputy Brigade Commander of the 235th Brigade of the same division. Resolution: Approved.

(1) Qin Zhen and others submitted a proposal to build a public cemetery for martyrs such as Tang Caichang, and to erect steles and pagodas at the locations where the martyrs were martyred, in order to make them immortal. It is requested that the central government and the local governments of Hubei and Hunan each bear one-third, which is 10,000 silver dollars. Please review and implement. Resolution: Approved. A letter will also be sent in reply to President Qu and Vice President of the Supervisory Yuan. Please instruct the Board of Directors of the Central Gengkuan Fund to also contact the Committee to borrow funds during the Committee's work period to facilitate progress. Resolution: Approved. Please review and issue orders to comply with the regulations. Resolution: Amended and approved, and forwarded to the National Government for record. The monthly operating expenses are 880 yuan, and the temporary relief expenses are 2,000 yuan. A budget estimate and a list of committee members have been prepared. Please review the case. Resolution: Approved. Please review the case. Resolution: Amended and approved. All military and political affairs will still be handled by the Silun Kasha. Please report to the central government to verify the telegram. Resolution: Approved. Japanese and Russian Defense Military Preparations 28

Have Changed to Take Offensive Plans

Minister of the Army Hayashi Said So in the House of Representatives

Foreign Minister Hirota Believes Russia's Words and Actions Are Gradually Easing

(Tokyo) The General Budget Committee of the House of Representatives opened at 10:35 a.m. today. Long Erdao, President of the Seiyukai, questioned the international situation after Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations. Foreign Minister Hirota explained Japan's relations with China, Russia, and the United States, saying that

Regarding the Russian issue, we plan to gradually resolve important issues between the two countries. We are currently striving to mediate the China Eastern Railway issue. Although relations with China cannot be resolved immediately, the government hopes that they will improve. As for diplomatic work with the United States, if there is a way to reassure the people of both Japan and the United States, it will be implemented immediately. Both Japan and the United States have no intention of creating incidents. Although the method and timing of the treaty between the two countries are not convenient to announce, the government is conducting this diplomatic work as a matter of fact. Long Erdao asked

Japan's relations with Russia have undergone major changes. Does the government have any intention of preventing the deterioration of people's hearts? Foreign Minister Hirota replied

The reason for the change in Japanese-Russian relations lies in the border defense issue. Japan intends to agree with the countries concerned on a treaty restricting border defense. Recently, Soviet Russia's words and actions have gradually eased. First resolve the important outstanding cases, and then we can obtain the stability of the people's hearts of the two countries. Nagaoka asked

The Soviet Union's movement of troops and transportation of military equipment seem to exceed the limits of border defense. Is this a fact? Minister of the Army Hayashi replied

The border defense between Japan and Russia is of course aimed at defensive posture, but it is not without consideration of taking the offensive. Long Erdao then mentioned Sino-Japanese relations, saying

Today is the best time to start Sino-Japanese negotiations. Does the government have the intention to actively carry out Sino-Japanese diplomatic work? Foreign Minister Hirota replied

It is necessary for China and Japan to establish friendly relations, but today is not the time to actively carry out it. We must wait for China's self-awareness, but this is not to say that we are bystanders. Long Erdao asked

Is there a continuing trend in the current world trade war? The Foreign Minister replied

The distorted state of world trade will not stop for the time being. Long Erdao asked

What about British-Japanese economic relations? The Foreign Minister replied

The political and diplomatic relations between the two countries are now quite optimistic, so resolving the international issues between the two countries in terms of commerce is the most necessary thing to maintain the friendly relations between the two countries. When it came to noon, the chairman announced a recess. In the afternoon, they concentrated on the General Budget Committee and reopened at 1:30 p.m. Long Erdao continued to question diplomatic issues, and advocated establishing British-Japanese diplomacy, improving the nature of diplomats in the era of economic diplomacy, and revising the establishment of diplomatic institutions. Foreign Minister Hirota agreed with him. In order to break through the diplomatic difficulties, Long Erdao declared that it is necessary to unify the national opinion and question the Foreign Minister. Foreign Minister Hirota replied

I also strongly support national diplomacy. Since taking office, I have explained the concept of the Japanese people to foreign countries, placing its emphasis on this. I am currently working hard to carry it out, because the keynote of the diplomatic policy is nothing more than this. Long Erdao asked

Regarding the major situations of diplomacy, national defense, finance, and economy, what is the Prime Minister's view on handling them well with the cooperation of the entire country and the cabinet? Prime Minister Saito replied

I fully express my agreement. Then, Tanaka Kou of the Minseito Party raised a question

Can the old market be exercised with the principle of imperial coordination? Foreign Minister Hirota replied

I think it should be carried out on the basis of reciprocal relations. Tanaka asked

Do you intend to impose retaliatory tariffs on countries that impose improper tariffs? The Foreign Minister replied

I intend to seek ad hoc disposition, and this matter is still under study. Tanaka said that concluding the Japanese-Indian trade treaty is unfavorable, and attacked the Foreign Minister, saying

Does the Foreign Minister think that the Japanese-Indian trade treaty is a success? The Foreign Minister replied

I don't think it is satisfactory. Minister of Commerce Nakajima also replied

Of course, it cannot be said to be a success. Tanaka also asked

What is our countermeasure to the establishment of tariff barriers by various countries? The Foreign Minister replied

This is a major issue, and the government is not in a position to publish the considerations hastily. Tanaka also asked the Director of the Commerce Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Kurosuke, about the exchange rate issue of the Japanese-Indian agreement, asking

Is there any intention to abrogate the new cotton cloth agreement? In the government, in the event of an emergency, is there a final determination to reform it? The Foreign Minister replied

The government's future policy is not convenient to state clearly, but I feel that there is a need to promote its establishment as much as possible. Tanaka asked again

What I am asking is not this, but asking about the government's determination. Please explain it clearly. The Prime Minister stood up and replied

The government is prepared to work hard to thoroughly implement the measures. After Tanaka raised various questions to the Minister of Agriculture, Representative Kazutami from the Seiyukai raised questions focusing on rural issues and social policies, and the meeting adjourned near six o'clock. (Jiji News Agency, 30th)

Future Great War Prediction 29

(Paris) The famous predictor Professor Remon declared today that the United States and Japan will go to war in 1946, but in 1935, Japan and Russia will inevitably have a war. He also said that when Japan, the United States, and Russia dispute in the future, the European countries will remain neutral. He also predicted that a ship will sink in the Atlantic Ocean this year, and there will be a train accident in Wahiawa, Hawaii. There will be three train accidents in France, one in Romania, and a submarine accident in Britain this year. There will be earthquakes in the United States, Italy, Cuba, Japan, China, Java, and Sumatra this year. The League of Nations will continue and there will be a phenomenon that all civilized countries in the world can enter it again. German Hitler can remain in place within this decade, and the Soviet Russian government can continue to move forward, but gradually tend to capitalism. (National Telegram, 30th)

A Great War Breaks Out in the Pacific

Our Country Will Inevitably Be Involved in the Vortex 30

Yan Huiqing Comments on Britain and Japan Competing for the Far East Market

Hishikari Said That the Red Army Has Deployed an Outer Line Encirclement

(Nanjing) Regarding the foreign situation, Ambassador Yan Huiqing has passed through Hong Kong and is heading north, and is expected to arrive in Shanghai and transfer to Nanjing around the 3rd of next month. (Special Dispatch, 30th)

(London) The London Daily Telegraph today published in large font a piece from its Singapore correspondent with the opinion of Dr. Yan Huiqing, the Chinese Minister to Russia. Dr. Yan believes that the next world war will take place in the Pacific, and the competition between Britain and Japan for the Far East market will be the cause of the next war. Russia is not yet prepared for war. Even if Japan provokes it, the Soviet Union will not rush to war due to the situation. He fears that any dispute in the Pacific will inevitably involve China. He believes that Japan's ambition is now focused on the oil-rich region of eastern Siberia. (Reuters, 30th)

(New York) The New York Times published an article by Crocker, commenting on the issue of the Japanese-Russian War, stating that the United States Army and Navy authorities deeply believe that the outbreak of the Japanese-Russian War is only a matter of time. At present, the construction of double tracks on the Siberian Railway has not yet been completed. Once the war starts, the Soviet Union can only transport 300 troops to eastern Siberia every day, which is beneficial for waiting. If Japan can delay the start of the war for a year or more, the Soviet Union's railway construction project will definitely progress, and Russia will also be able to send a considerable number of reinforcements to Siberia. The new Japanese Minister of the Army, General Hayashi, is well aware of this, but would rather wait, because once the war breaks out, Russian planes can fly out of Vladivostok and bomb the industrial centers of Japan, such as Tokyo, Osaka, and Yokohama. The Soviet Air Force has a formidable reputation, and Japan has no ability to resist it. In addition, according to news received from Washington, the situation occupied by the Japanese in "Manchukuo" does not seem as solid as it appears on the surface. Even in the "future emperor" Puyi, there are also some difficulties. This is another reason for Japan's caution, and so on. (Havas, 30th)

(Dalian) Hishikari, Commander of the Kwantung Army, arrived in Dalian at 7:20 p.m. on the 29th with staff officer Tatsumi, adjutant Reigang, secretary Tsurumi, secretary Shiohara, and Captain Kishi of the Military Police to inspect the affairs of the Kwantung Government. They immediately took a car to the official residence in Lushun. There are considerable actions in Vladivostok, all the way to Daury and the Red Army base. It is impossible to know whether these military preparations are for defense or attack, because they are the intentions of the Red Army. Therefore, we should be most cautious about occasional incidents in the future. From this, we can know that Soviet Russia misunderstands Japan's true intentions. If the Japanese can travel to Moscow one after another to carry out the so-called national diplomacy, it seems to be very meaningful to ease the atmosphere. (Special Dispatch, 30th)

Responding to the Far East Incident

US to Add 1,000 Aircraft, Requiring 90 Million Gold Dollars 34

Naval Affairs Committee Passes Vinson Amendment

Authorizing the President to Expand Air Force Strength

Submitted to the House of Representatives for Discussion Yesterday

(Washington) The House Naval Affairs Committee unanimously passed Mr. Vinson's proposal to purchase 1,184 naval aircraft, along with amendments. Thus, the bill has good prospects for passage in Congress. The House will discuss the bill tomorrow. Currently, both the House and Senate have no objections to the proposal. The amendment appropriates 90 million dollars and authorizes the President to add aircraft to complete the naval plan. According to Vice Admiral Standley, the Washington Conference stipulated that the navy could have 2,184 aircraft. The United States currently has only 1,000, so 1,184 more are needed. 650 of these are already under construction, and the remaining 534 will be rushed into production as soon as the proposal and amendments are passed. If Mr. Vinson's proposal and amendments are passed, the strength of the US Navy and Air Force can be expanded to the stipulated number. The naval budget bill has already passed for the addition of one 8-inch gunboat and three 6-inch gun cruisers, and the expansion of the navy to 81,500 personnel and the Marine Corps to 16,000. Repairs will be made to old warships, and 102 warships must be added within five years according to Mr. Vinson's proposal. Furthermore, the US Navy Department announced this week a "Naval Five-Year Plan," and the previous proposal to add 1,184 aircraft may be based on this. (29th National Telegraph)

Britain Sends Note to Seven Governments

Endorsing German Military Equality 35

Suggesting a Compromise Solution

Reconciling Franco-German Differences

Mussolini's Sympathy Undoubted

Fate Hinges on US Attitude

(London) The contents of the British memorandum on disarmament have been revealed today. It is reported that Britain has formally informed the countries concerned of its recognition of Germany's right to equality in armaments. The countries that received the memorandum include Germany, the United States, France, Italy, Japan, Belgium, and Poland. Its content includes Britain's fundamental position on important armament issues, with the main points as follows: (1) Proposing the absolute elimination or reduction of offensive weapons. (2) Equality of armaments, meaning Britain promotes the abolition of the probationary period under the management of various countries and recognizes that Germany should immediately obtain equality in national defense armaments. The fate of the memorandum will depend entirely on the attitude of the United States, as its content proposed referring to the Kellogg Pact's provisions for resolving international disputes. Germany's disarmament and probationary period have long been France's demand for security. If the United States agrees with Britain's proposal, all parties are confident that France will concede. Since Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations, France has already made significant concessions, but the extent to which it will concede is still difficult to predict. German Chancellor Hitler demands Germany's rearmament, arguing that the weakness of Germany's current armaments is a major obstacle to the future of European peace, as neighboring countries will take the opportunity to invade. It is widely believed that this British memorandum will be strongly supported by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, as he previously stated that allowing Germany's military equality is an obligation of international morality. (30th National Telegraph)

(London) According to well-informed reporters, Britain's mediation plan will firmly reject the claim for a probationary period and propose that Germany be allowed to possess defensive weapons based on the principle of rights, and propose that the number of such weapons should be determined in later negotiations. (29th National Telegraph)

Key Points of the British Compromise Plan 36

Simultaneously Addressing Disarmament, Equality, and Security

Maintaining the Supervisory System, the Probationary Period Renamed Transition

(Paris) According to well-informed sources in London, the method stated in the British memorandum is to seek a compromise between Germany's armament demands and France's security demands according to the main principles. The main principles are three: disarmament, armament, equality, and security. As for the controversial "disarmament probationary period," it is renamed "transition period." During this period, countries should reduce offensive weapons, but Germany should obtain some samples of such weapons. Regarding the issue of troop numbers, Germany demands 300,000, while the MacDonald plan stipulates 200,000. This memorandum seeks a compromise number between the two. Regarding the issue of security, the supervisory system is still maintained, but it must be implemented universally in all countries so that Germany will no longer have grievances. The memorandum also argues that if Germany violates its promises, the countries of the disarmament convention should consult each other and may suspend their own obligations under the convention. (29th Havas Telegraph)

British Note Delivered to French and German Governments 37

(Berlin) British Ambassador Sir Eric Phipps paid a visit to Chancellor Hitler this afternoon and personally handed over the memorandum of the British government's final note to Germany. Foreign Minister Neurath was also present. It is said that the so-called German final note is Germany's request for Britain to put forward new suggestions, hoping to find a compromise between the French memorandum and the Berlin reply. (29th Havas Telegraph)

(Paris) This evening, the British Chargé d'Affaires in Paris, Campbell, met with the Secretary-General of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Léger. It is assumed that Campbell has delivered the disarmament memorandum announced by British Foreign Secretary Simon to the House of Commons to the Ministry. (29th Havas)

British White Paper to be Published Tomorrow 38

Official Circles Temporarily Silent

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon made a speech in the House of Commons yesterday on the issue of disarmament, saying that the government will publish a white paper to accurately explain the British government's policy on the issue of disarmament. This white paper is now scheduled to be published on Thursday. (30th Havas Telegraph)

(London) Official circles are unwilling to criticize the content of the British disarmament memorandum, but reliable sources say that Britain is now acting as a mediator again. Although Franco-German negotiations have broken down, the desire of both countries to reach a solution is more urgent than before. France can certainly appeal to the League of Nations, but the result of this move will ultimately be the failure of the main body of the disarmament conference. Direct Franco-German negotiations do not seem to be the right time now. In order to promote mediation, the British memorandum will definitely put forward new disarmament methods and be accepted by people. Britain's previous proposals have been well received by the countries concerned, and the new proposals are even more advanced than the previous ones. (30th Reuters Telegraph)

British Parliament Convenes 39

Simon Explains:

Clarifying the Urgent Need for Disarmament

No Criticism of the Pseudo-Reform System

(London) The British House of Commons reconvened today after the Christmas holiday. Labour Party leader Lansbury was absent due to illness, so the opposition party is temporarily led by Attlee. Foreign Secretary Simon recounted his conversations with Mussolini, Schuschnigg, and Benckendorff, saying that this discussion greatly helped clarify the issue of disarmament and establish points of agreement. The British government also obtained more detailed information from diplomatic channels about Germany's statements after Hitler's withdrawal from the disarmament conference. As a result, the British government decided that it was now time to announce its attitude on this important issue. Britain has sent a memorandum to the countries most recently involved in the discussion, and the original text will be published later. The British government believes that any issue concerning the improvement of the League of Nations is secondary to the more urgent issue of disarmament. France and Italy share this view. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has stated that the purpose of his proposal to improve the League of Nations is to consolidate the League of Nations' institutions and make them more effective. Britain does not want to take any action on this matter until the disarmament negotiations have yielded results. Simon also briefly mentioned the Far East incident and the rebellion in Fujian Province, saying that the Chinese government's friendly acceptance of the British note requesting protection of British lives and property in Fujian Province was quite gratifying. Simon then mentioned the news of Puyi's enthronement, but did not criticize it. Many members of the House of Commons inquired about the progress of the British-Japanese cotton industry discussions. Overseas Trade Minister Colville answered them one by one, saying that the discussion must also include the rayon industry, which is very clear and should not give rise to any objections. He hopes that the discussion can be successful quickly, and the government does not impose any time limit on the negotiations. (29th Reuters Telegraph)

Since the Establishment of the British Government

Facing the Most Critical Period 40

(London) According to the opinion of the general public in London, after the Parliament reconvenes today, the British government will enter the most critical period since its establishment. The Socialist Party has announced that a general election will be held this year, but the government seems to have no reason to step down before 1936. However, every government must undergo a major test in its third year. Now, both friends and enemies of the government are demanding that the government adopt a bolder attitude on many issues. Many people, especially on the disarmament issue, believe that only if Britain takes a firm stance can the debate on peace and war be decided. At the same time, opponents of the government are clamoring that Britain has reduced its armaments to the point where they cannot be reduced any further, so how can it expect foreign countries to pay attention? As for the government's attitude towards disarmament, it is already well-prepared, and its nature can only be expressed after foreign governments have studied its stated aspirations. It is expected that the government, in addition to the questions it must answer in the House of Commons today, will also be forced to deal with issues such as reforming the League of Nations, resisting Japanese trade competition, and assisting the British shipping industry. The Socialist Party is also prepared to fight unremittingly for the unemployment insurance bill. According to the phenomena, the whole country is already tired of the old party struggles, and the true meaning of the national unity government is also nearly vague. Therefore, there is a demand to absorb the steady elements of the Conservative Party, the Liberal Party, and the Labour Party, who are not entirely satisfied with the current government. However, in view of the Socialist Party's or the Fascist dictatorship's intimidation, they want to embark on a dangerous path again. (29th Reuters Telegraph)

Concentrating Talents, a New French Cabinet is Formed

Daladier is Premier and Foreign Minister 41

Swiftly and Firmly as Guiding Principles

Thoroughly Reforming Finances as its Duty

(Paris) Former Prime Minister Daladier, the resigning Minister of the Army, was ordered by President Lebrun to form a new cabinet, and has now succeeded. Its list is as follows: Prime Minister Daladier, concurrently Minister of Foreign Affairs; Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs, Marie (Secretary-General of the Council of State in the Sarraut Cabinet); Minister of Justice, Berthon (Minister of Justice in Daladier's first cabinet); Minister of the Interior, Frot (Minister of Labour in the Chautemps Cabinet); Undersecretary of the Interior, Heraud (Member of Parliament); Minister of Finance and Budget, Pietri (Minister of Colonies in the Sarraut Cabinet); Minister of the Army, Fabry (Member of Parliament); Minister of Agriculture, Queuille (unchanged); Minister of Aviation, Cot (unchanged); Minister of Colonies, Jeanneney (Senator, former Ambassador to Italy); Minister of Commerce, Mistler (Minister of Posts and Telecommunications in the Chautemps Cabinet); Minister of the Navy, Champetier de Ribes (Member of Parliament); Secretary-General of the Council of State, Marnot de Sainte Marie (Member of Parliament). (30th Havas Telegraph)

(Paris) The new Prime Minister Daladier declared that the new cabinet's guiding principles are swiftness and firmness. The first cabinet meeting has already been held this afternoon. Daladier also issued a declaration stating that the budget bill must be voted on before the end of March, and the national expenditure system must be thoroughly reformed. He also said that the restoration of confidence and the settlement of finances are necessary conditions for the success of foreign policy. Judging from this, the new cabinet does have an air of swiftness and firmness. Daladier has brought together the left, the center, and the right, and has excluded all extremists in the parliament, which is unprecedented. The characteristics of the new cabinet are: Béranger, Chairman of the Senate Civil and Criminal Legislation Committee, as Minister of Justice, who will handle the Stavisky suicide investigation thoroughly; Fabry as Minister of the Army, who is a loyal member of the right wing and the editor-in-chief of L'Action Française; Pietri as Minister of Finance, who is a recognized expert and known for his loyalty; and the Ministry of Colonies is now renamed the Ministry of Overseas Territories, and the minister is Senator Jeanneney, who is also highly talented. Daladier's self-appointment as Minister of Foreign Affairs can make the cabinet's work particularly smooth, as he has long held this position and has a strong view on the necessity of direct Franco-German understanding. (30th Reuters Telegraph)

The party found it inconvenient to join the new cabinet. This decision was subsequently passed by a vote of thirteen to nine. (30th Havas Telegraph)

The Establishment of the Balkan Pact

Many Twists and Turns Still Lie Ahead 51

Bulgaria Can Hardly Accept the Border Security Issue

Foreign Ministers of the Little Entente Will Continue Consultations

Capital of Yugoslavia 52

The King of Bulgaria, accompanied by the Prime Minister, was in the capital to discuss the issue of a non-aggression treaty between the Balkan countries with the Romanian authorities. The general public originally thought that as a result of the talks, this treaty would not be difficult to establish quickly. Looking at the current situation, I am afraid that this hope cannot be realized. Responsible people here also said that it is too early to say that the Balkan Treaty can be signed on the second of next month. The draft treaty originally drafted by Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu and Greek Foreign Minister Maximos has been amended after the meeting of the Foreign Ministers of the Little Entente countries in Zagreb, Yugoslavia, and the talks between Bulgaria and Romania. The parties concerned cannot agree on everything, and there are still areas for consultation. Therefore, the Foreign Ministers of Greece, Romania, and Turkey are scheduled to arrive here on the second of next month to renegotiate with Yugoslav Foreign Minister Jevtić. Bulgaria originally did not object in principle to the Balkan Non-Aggression Treaty. However, the draft treaty stipulates that the contracting states shall mutually guarantee territorial security and border security, which is tantamount to adding another layer of guarantee to the Peace Treaty, which Bulgaria is dissatisfied with. This is precisely why Bulgaria does not want to participate in the new Balkan Convention. When the Foreign Ministers of Greece, Romania, Turkey, and Yugoslavia meet at the beginning of next month, they will first discuss this complex border security issue, and Yugoslavia in particular wants to find a way to make Bulgaria recognize it. (29th Havas Telegraph)

Britain and the United States Have Not Reached an Understanding

Currency War is Almost Inevitable 53

Informal Negotiations are Underway

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau said today that he will soon begin currency talks with Britain. According to responsible sources, the Treasury Department has not reached an understanding with London on the relationship between the pound and the dollar. Since the Treasury Department intends to use its newly established 200 million dollar equalization fund, a fierce currency war may be unavoidable. Morgenthau openly admitted that he did not know whether a currency war was about to break out, but others believed that it was inevitable. The House of Representatives unanimously agreed to the Senate's amendment to the currency bill. Tonight, Congress may send this bill to President Roosevelt, who will immediately issue a proclamation ordering that the value of the dollar be reduced by 40 percent. (29th Reuters Telegraph)

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau, after accepting the Senate's amendment to the currency bill in the House of Representatives today, replied to questions from members of Congress, saying that we are not currently having any discussions with Britain, but if someone asks about this again next week, he will not be willing to answer. Morgenthau also said that he has prepared several orders for managing gold, and the government will issue them after the President approves the currency bill. When asked about a currency war, Morgenthau smiled and replied that both sides must pay a heavy price for such a war. He also said that the Federal Reserve Bank of New York will continue to operate the equalization fund as an agency of the Treasury Department. The Wall Street Journal said that formal negotiations to maintain the status quo are currently underway, and the pound will be temporarily stabilized at a price of four dollars and seventy-five cents for a six-cornered dollar. (29th Reuters Telegraph)

The USSR balloon is 180 feet high and is the largest in the world. It only took forty-five minutes to ascend before breaking Professor Picard's record of 53,151 feet in Belgium. International Second Polar Year

Our Country's Meteorological Observation Report 63

(Nanjing) The International Meteorological Society previously decided that August 1, 1932 to August 31, 1933 would be the International Second Polar Year. It invited meteorological stations from various countries to conduct observations near the North and South Poles, or to establish weather stations on high mountains and ridges. With the assistance of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture, the Central Meteorological Research Institute of our country also purchased instruments and established weather stations on the Jade Emperor Peak of Mount Tai in Shandong and the Thousand Buddha Peak of Mount Emei in Sichuan. The following results were obtained from thirteen months of observation during the Polar Year: (1) The abundance of rainfall on the summit of Mount Emei. During the Polar Year, a total of 9226 millimeters of rainfall was recorded, which is equivalent to ten years' worth of rainfall in the Beijing-Shanghai area. (2) The annual air pressure on Mount Emei is low in winter and high in summer. On the plains, the air pressure in various parts of our country is high in winter and low in summer, which creates a monsoon climate. However, the air pressure variation on Mount Emei is high in summer and low in winter. (3) The temperature on Mount Emei in winter is higher than that on Mount Tai. Mount Emei is about 1,800 meters higher than Mount Tai, but the temperature in winter is actually higher than that on Mount Tai. (4) There are no monsoons on Mount Emei throughout the year. The winter monsoon has disappeared on Mount Tai, but there is still a summer monsoon. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Guangdong Authorities Proceed with Aviation Network 82

It is said that two of them have already arrived in Hong Kong, so the line can be completed in February. The line will temporarily terminate at Longzhou, and then expand to Yunnanfu and Chongqing in Western Sichuan. The official date of formal establishment is said to be February 2. At that time, a plane will fly from Hankou to the provincial capital, and then fly from here to Xi'an on February 6. Afterwards, there will be one flight to Xi'an and two flights to Hankou every week. The authorities have requested the local authorities along the route of the aircraft to provide effective protection and take care of everything. (30th Reuters Dispatch)

Chen Jitang Actively

Deploys Guangdong Border Defense 92

Large Army Opens to the Fujian-Guangdong Border

Airfields Massively Expanded

Coastal Defenses Also Established in Shantou

Shantou correspondence: After the defeat of the 19th Route Army in Fujian, Chen Jitang immediately transferred a large army to the Fujian-Guangdong border. Currently, Deng Longguang's and Li Genliang's divisions and Chen Zhang's brigade are defending the three counties of Dapu, Yongding, and Pinghe. Chen also appointed Fan Zongchi, former regimental commander of the 19th Route Army, to enter Fujian with Deng Longguang's division. Chen Weiyuan, former brigade commander of the 19th Route Army, was also appointed Commander of the Southern Fujian Garrison. Chen left Shantou on the 25th and entered Zhao'an via Raoping. Chen, originally from Fujian, has considerable connections with Zhang Zhen's old troops. His purpose in entering Fujian is to recruit the local armies of various counties in southern Fujian, and at the same time, to enlist stray troops from the 19th Route Army to return. After entering Fujian, Chen will set up an office between Pinghe, Yunxiao, and Zhangpu. The division commanders of the stationed troops on the Fujian-Guangdong border have returned to the province in recent days at the invitation of Chen Jitang to discuss key border defense issues of Fujian and Jiangxi. Huang Renhuan, Zhang Ruigui, and Huang Yanzhen are all in Guangzhou. Liu Shunan's regiment, the 14th Regiment of Li Zhenliang's division, passed through Xingning and entered Fenglang in Dapu on the 23rd. Ma Yi, of the 13th Regiment, opened to Sanheba from Wuhua on the 26th. Li Zhenliang and the division headquarters' special service battalion moved entirely to Dapu on the 27th. Luo Xiuli's 15th Regiment was also transported from Shanwei to Shantou in succession aboard the HaiRui and HaiZhou warships, and then transferred to Raoping Shangrao to guard Tiger Pass. It is said that Li's division is going to Yongding and Pinghe, so in recent days, the counties in the upper reaches of the Han River have been extremely busy hiring laborers. Each county has been ordered to recruit 200 people, and each police district has been ordered to search for recruits from the public. Deng Longguang's division stationed in Huizhou also moved out on the 23rd. Pan Biao, the first regimental commander, Tang Fu, the second regimental commander, Zhao Lan, the third regimental commander, Lu Haodong, the fourth regimental commander, and Wang Dequan, the training regimental commander, all started from Heyuan, Laolong, Zijin, Wuhua, and Xingning counties and advanced. They concentrated in Meixian on the 27th and advanced to Guanshi in Jiaoling Wuping Shanghang. The various units of Miao Peinan's division, the first regiment, Chen Cequn, and the third regiment, Chen Qijie, and the training regiment of the Second Army, Zhang Wei's troops, also filled the defense along the Dong River. It is also said that Chen Zhang's brigade will be transferred from the North River to the upper reaches of the East River, Heping Longchuan, and even to the Fujian border. At present, the defensive works in the various counties on the Guangdong border have been completely completed, and road traffic is also very convenient. Xingning Jiaoling Raoping on the route from Guangzhou to the Fujian-Jiangxi border can all be reached in one day. It only takes six hours to travel from Chaoshan Jieyang to Xingning, and there are also a large number of cars for transportation. Chen Jitang previously purchased 50 large cars from Hong Kong, and 20 of them have arrived on the eastern route and are being used for military purposes. The Meixian airfield has been expanded to twice its size at Gutangping since the plane accident, forming a human-shaped airfield that can accommodate the take-off and landing of 30 aircraft. Hangars, oil depots, anti-aircraft guns, listening devices, and searchlights are all available. The layout is even better than that of the Shantou airfield, with a model of an air force base. There are also airfields in Jiaoling and Xingning, but they are not as grand as the one in Meixian. Chen Jitang also ordered the counties of Chaozhou and Meizhou to form 100 companies of people's reserve teams, each team with 30 people. All guns and artillery are supplied by the headquarters and are responsible for bandit defense. The Fengshun County police force has been allocated 20 mortars, as well as a number of machine guns and rifles, from the headquarters. In addition, Guangdong Province has recently been actively deploying for coastal defense. Zhang Zhiying, commander of the Shantou and Shanwei coastal naval fortress, is responsible for the equipment. Zhang has ordered four of the latest type of torpedoes from the Vickers shipyard in England, each costing 500,000 Hong Kong dollars. The first and second torpedoes have already been delivered, and Zhang has appointed Zou Wenguang as the captain of the first ship and Liang Kangnian as the captain of the second ship. The third and fourth ships will also be delivered during the day and will be stationed in Shantou and Qiongzhou. Secondly, six new-style 1,000-ton miniature gunboats have been ordered from England, which can sail on both rivers and seas. In addition, 20,000 steel helmets, searchlights, iron arrow silk, and various other large quantities of military supplies have been purchased in Hong Kong. He is very excited about the deployment of the Fujian-Jiangxi border defense.

The Question of Inner Mongolia's Request for Autonomy (Continued) 93

Mongolians Still Hold Objections to Central Government Regulations

D. The Relationship Between Leagues and Provinces: The League Headquarters is built above the Banner, and the Province is built above the County, so the League Headquarters and the Province are also a dual organization in the same place, only differing in the size of their area. For example, the Xilingol League governs ten Banners, the Chahar League governs twelve Banners, the Ulanqab League governs six Banners, the Ikh Juu League governs seven Banners, and Tumet is a special Banner. The Chahar and Suiyuan Provinces govern the ten counties north of the Great Wall that were transferred from Hebei, and the six counties established in the four Banners and four groups of the left wing of the Chahar League, respectively. The Suiyuan Province governs the eighteen counties established in the four Banners of the right wing of the Ulanqab League, the Ikh Juu League, the Tumet Banner, and the Chahar League. The League Headquarters and the Provinces are all directly under the central government. The position of the League Headquarters has not changed due to the establishment of Provinces. Therefore, the five counties of Taolin and Jining, etc., established in the four Banners of the right wing of the Chahar League, are under the jurisdiction of Suiyuan Province, but the four Banners still belong to the Chahar League. This proves that the Provinces and Counties and the League Headquarters and Banners each form a system. In the event of matters involving mutual affairs, they shall be handled through consultation. This is the fact. The organization law of the League Headquarters and Banners also has clear provisions. However, conflicts often arise when the Provinces and Counties encroach on the League Banners. E. The Reclamation and Preservation of Land: Mongolian land was originally the natural pasture of the Mongolian people. Since the free migration of people from the interior and the forced reclamation of land by the Mongolian border Provinces and Counties, Mongolians who cannot be changed into farmers have been greatly affected in their livelihoods. After the reclamation, the provincial and county governments did not allocate the land price that the Mongolian Banner should have received and the annual land rent that should have been divided according to the original regulations, which made the administrative expenses of the League Banner also feel difficult. If this continues, the League Banner and the Mongolian people will likely perish together. Therefore, the Mongol officials and people are all in fear when they hear the sound of reclamation. At present, the advocacy of reserving uncultivated Mongolian land as pasture for the Mongolian people, improving animal husbandry, starting ancillary industries, and developing the local economy, and that even cultivation must be according to the convenience of the Mongolian people, has become a general appeal of Mongolia. As for the issue of land owner and tenant rights of Mongolian and Han people in the cultivated areas, disputes and lawsuits are constantly occurring. As a result, most Mongolians fail, and national feelings are also affected. Therefore, stopping the reclamation of Mongolian pastureland and reorganizing the cultivated land have become urgent issues on the Mongolian border today. F. The Collection and Division of Taxes: The income of uncultivated Mongolian land has always been managed by the Mongolian Banner. The Mongolian Banner also collects taxes on cultivated land. For example, the Ulanqab League and the Ikh Juu League collect Mongolian rent and water grass fees from the reclaimers within their borders, and coal rent and taxes from the coal mines. The Banners of the Chahar League collect the four-percent private rent from the reclaimers within their borders. All these are rents and taxes collected by the Mongolian Banner in its capacity as a landlord. All the administrative expenses of the League Banner are also maintained by this. In addition, the collection bureaus set up by the Provinces and Counties in the Mongolian Banner also allocate a certain amount to the Mongolian Banner. For example, the Suiyuan Province allocates thousands of yuan to the Darhan Banner every year from the Baolingu Temple Tax Bureau. This kind of collection or division is especially common in eastern Mongolia. However, the Provinces and Counties often infringe on and withhold this tax revenue of the Mongolian Banner. For example, after the Ziyou County collected the four-percent private rent that the Banners of the Chahar League should have received, it has not allocated a single penny for many years. The resentment of the Mongolian people arises from this. Therefore, protecting the inherent rent and taxes of the Mongolian Banner and properly setting the tax-sharing method with the Provinces are also major issues on the Mongolian border today. (II) The Process and Key Points of the Autonomy Method Agreed Upon at Baolingu Temple: In the autumn of last year, the heads and representatives of the Mongolian Leagues and Banners gathered at Baolingu Temple to request autonomy. There were two purposes: (1) To unite the Leagues and Banners and special Banners, which have always governed themselves separately, in order to jointly resist foreign aggression. (2) To eliminate the disputes between the League Banners and the Provincial Counties, so as to avoid the danger of evolving into ethnic struggles in the future. Therefore, the Baolingu Temple Autonomy Conference initially advocated abolishing the Mongolian border provinces and establishing an entire Inner Mongolian Autonomous Government, acting under the central government, to govern all Inner Mongolian Banners and Counties, for Mongolians and Han to cooperate and jointly resist foreign aggression. It also drafted thirty-six articles of the Organizational Law of the Inner Mongolian Autonomous Government at the conference and sent them to Minister Huang when he arrived at Baolingu Temple, requesting that they be forwarded to the central government. On the Mongolian side in Baolingu Temple, this was called a high degree of autonomy. Minister Huang did not accept it because the abolition of the border provinces involved too much. In order to respect the wishes of the central government officials, the heads and representatives of the various Leagues and Banners in Baolingu Temple, after several days of discussion, proposed eleven other methods, advocating that the entire Inner Mongolian Autonomous Government should still be established, but its powers should be reduced to exclusively governing the Leagues and Banners, while the Mongolian border Provinces would still exist and exclusively govern their respective Counties. However, it would be necessary to clearly divide the powers and revenues between the Provincial Counties and the League Banners, stop the reclamation, and not establish any more Counties. For the existing Provincial Counties, they would cooperate. On the Mongolian side in Baolingu Temple, this was called a medium degree of autonomy. After this method was sent to Minister Huang by the delegates sent by the Presidium of the Autonomy Conference on November 16, Minister Huang sent Li Songfeng and others to discuss with Su Ludai and others sent by the Presidium. As a result, this method was not accepted because the first article still advocated organizing the entire Autonomous Government, which was inconsistent with the principle decided by the central government that Mongolian autonomy should be based on the Province. On the morning of November 17, Minister Huang announced his departure from Mongolia and his return to the south, expressing his finality. For the sake of seeking compromise, the heads and representatives of the various Leagues and Banners, after repeated discussions, and by midnight, changed the first article of the previously sent method into two methods: (A) Establishing the First and Second Autonomous Region Governments to govern the various League Banners, respectively. (B) Establishing the entire Mongolian Autonomous Committee to exclusively govern the various League Banners.

On the Mongolian side in Baolingu Temple, these two were called a low degree of autonomy. After this method was sent to Minister Huang for adoption of one of the two, Minister Huang expressed his acceptance of method A when he met with the Presidium of the Autonomy Conference on the morning of the 18th. As for the ten articles below the second article of the previously sent method, the Presidium also requested that they be completed, and Minister Huang agreed to do his best. In the afternoon, Li Songfeng and others designated by Minister Huang and Su Ludai and others designated by the Presidium studied this method article by article, and no objections were raised. This is what is called the eleven articles of the autonomy method agreed upon at Baolingu Temple. The key points of the second and subsequent articles of the method were the two items of stopping the release of pastureland and dividing the tax revenue. Therefore, in the telegram of thanks to the central government from the Presidium, in addition to stating the method of regional autonomy, there were also the words "Regarding the cases of stopping the release of pastureland and dividing local tax revenue, they are also allowed to be handled as much as possible." The draft of the telegram had been reviewed by Minister Huang, so the Mongolian side believed that Minister Huang had accepted this method.

Yellow River Flood Prevention Conference in Henan Province 94

Five Important Resolutions Passed

Kaifeng Dispatch: The Henan Province Yellow River flood prevention conference was held this morning at 9:00 AM in the Construction Department. Attendees included Zhang Jingyu, Director of the Construction Department; Chen Ruzhen, Director of the River Affairs Bureau; Zhang Hanying, representative of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission; Chen Hefu, representative of the Huai River Regulation Commission; Su Jinren, representative of the Longhai Railway Bureau; Zhu Xianbin, representative of the Jinpu Railway Bureau; Gu Houxi, representative of the Jiangsu Provincial Government; Fan Jiatu, representative of the Anhui Provincial Government; as well as Xu Baikui, section chief of the Henan Construction Department, and Xie Zhian, technical expert. Zhang Jingyu chaired the meeting, with Dong Mingcheng as the recorder.

Following standard procedures, Chairman Zhang delivered a report, essentially stating that since the major flood in Henan last year, the foundations of the dikes have been severely eroded by the floodwaters. The works along the southern bank are especially dangerous. Chairman Liu of the province specially invited representatives from the Ministry and relevant provinces to jointly discuss how to prevent an unprecedented catastrophe. The discussion points can be divided into three aspects: engineering, transportation, and economics.

Next, the matters for discussion: (1) How should the construction principles for dangerous sections of the Yellow River in Henan Province be defined? Resolved: 1. The top of the dikes at dangerous sections should be raised to at least two meters above the 1933 flood level as the standard. 2. The width of the dike top should be at least 20 meters. 3. For dikes, the slope on the river side should be 1:3 above 5 meters, and 1:5 below (the principle for increasing the height and thickness of the dike body is to use silt). 4. Stone work, except for building groynes and revetments at necessary locations, should primarily focus on repairing old dikes. 5. Sufficient stone materials, earth bulls, and materials must be prepared at each dangerous section.

(2) How should the plans for dangerous sections be drafted? Resolved: The plans for dangerous sections should be based on the principles in the first resolution, with reference to the post-flood engineering plans of the River Affairs Bureau and the opinions of the Construction Department. The Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, the Henan Provincial Construction Department, and the River Affairs Bureau will jointly draft the plans, to be completed within two weeks. The Construction Department will be responsible for convening the meeting and each party will send a special representative.

(3) Regarding the transportation of materials needed for dangerous sections of the Yellow River in Henan Province to ensure speed, please discuss. Resolved: 1. The railway should provide free transportation of the required stone materials to the designated stations. 2. Request the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ministry of Railways to lend 180 li of narrow-gauge railway track and 300 dump trucks to the province for laying and transporting materials.

(4) How should the quantity and storage locations of stone materials be determined? Resolved: 1. Temporarily store 10,000 cubic meters in Kaifeng. Temporarily store 10,000 cubic meters in Zhongmou. Temporarily store 50,000 cubic meters in Zhengzhou and Rongze.

(5) How should the funding for the dangerous section projects be raised? Resolved: After the plans are drafted, Henan will consult with the customs, various ministries and commissions, and the provincial government to jointly raise the funds.

The meeting adjourned around 1:00 PM. (January 27th)

Secret Investigation by the Control Yuan into Lianshui Officials 95

| County Magistrate Chen Tongshou Accused by Citizens |

Songjiang

County Government Convenes River Dredging Conference 96

The city river in Songjiang has been in disrepair for many years, gradually silting up. The river water is murky, and at low tide, it is almost like a ditch, severely affecting drinking water and sanitation. From the beginning of his tenure, County Magistrate Jin considered river dredging to be an essential task, but due to the large scale of the project and high costs, it had not been undertaken. Now, with the start of the agricultural slack season, it is a good opportunity for river dredging. Therefore, County Magistrate Jin convened a meeting of local public organization leaders at the county government at 1:00 PM on the 30th to discuss river dredging.

County Magistrate Jin chaired the meeting, reported on the purpose of the meeting, and reported on the river dredging plan, budget, and survey situation in detail. More than 30 people attended, including Cai Zhongyu. The original plan was to dredge the city trunk river and estimated the cost at 48,000 yuan. Subsequently, attendees suggested that since a large-scale river dredging was underway, the tributary rivers connected to the trunk river, such as Bailongtan and Songjiaqiao, should also be dredged at the same time, otherwise the trunk river would easily silt up again even if it was dredged. The meeting resolved to reassess the total cost, which was estimated to be approximately 70,000 yuan, with half of the funds to be raised through donations. The county government would allocate 3,000 yuan from the construction fund, borrow 10,000 yuan from the seawall fund, and borrow 15,000 yuan from the 1934 construction fund. A remaining 7,000 yuan would be raised from the areas along the tributary roads.

With the funding secured, the meeting moved on to organizational matters. Nine people, including Cai Zhongyu and Wang Zhewu, were elected as standing committee members. Li Yangxian was appointed to the General Affairs Section, Li Jingxian to the Economic Section, Shen Lianbi to the Audit Section, and Xu Mojia to the Engineering Section, each taking on specific responsibilities. The meeting concluded after discussions and preparations. The county government will report the proceedings of today's meeting to the Provincial Construction Department for record-keeping and will immediately begin the work.

Bankruptcy Dispute of Renchangyu Cloth Shop in Suzhou 97

Renchangyu Cloth Shop, located on Shangtang Street outside Changmen, is an old shop with over 30 years of history. Recently, it suddenly went bankrupt. Wang Qianfu, the shareholder and manager of the shop, retained lawyer Lu Xiangru to announce the liquidation. It is rumored that the shop has debts of over 70,000 yuan. The creditors believe that the shop's business operations were not loss-making, but that the manager personally lost over 30,000 yuan, leading to a cash flow problem. Arrest of the Main Culprit in the Murder Case in Ximen, Wuxi 98

Chen Wang, the mistress of Chen Tingji Woodworks located in Li Lane near Baciao Bridge outside Ximen (57 years old), was suddenly attacked in the head with three axe blows and died at midnight on the 26th of this month. The murderer fled the scene. The next day, the fourth public security bureau in charge of the area, suspecting Chen Cuiyun, the daughter of the deceased, arrested her and brought her to the bureau for questioning. The head of the district also reported the situation of the autopsy to the court. Since the case occurred, Fan Xin, the director of the fourth public security bureau, immediately started the investigation and repeatedly questioned Chen Cuiyun, obtaining clues. Chen Qibao (also known as Feng Qibao), nephew of the deceased, was suspected of committing the murder. The night before, he personally led the police to Chen's house and arrested Qibao. Under Cuiyun's pillow, they found a letter from Chen Xueqin (also known as Cuiyun) to Feng Luan (also known as Qibao), a flashlight, and a pocket watch. Under the mattress, they found a dirty cloth stained with blood and yellow filth. He immediately took them to the bureau. Cuiyun and Qibao were interrogated separately and strictly. They confessed that Cuiyun and Qibao had an incestuous relationship. Because Chen Wang (the deceased) discovered the relationship, they planned the murder. A few days ago, Wang asked Qibao for four yuan and five jiao in membership fees, which led to an argument, so Qibao's murderous intent grew stronger. That night, he broke into the room with an axe, giving Wang three axe blows. Cuiyun had helped remove the window lock, etc. After receiving the confession, Director Fan believed that the truth was revealed and presented both criminals to the general bureau, and today transferred them to the county court for trial. It is said that Chen Qibao's killing of his aunt was not only due to the incestuous relationship with Cuiyun but also due to a dispute over inheritance.

An Elderly Man Died in a Fire 99

In the Hehua Pond area of Yangjiaqiao Township, District 8 of the county, Qian Sanquan, a 79-year-old villager, had three sons, all farmers, and a poor family. Father and sons were not harmonious. The other night, Sanquan took a bowl, filled it with rice husk ash, and placed it in his bedding as a foot warmer because of the cold weather. Inadvertently, he knocked the bowl over, scorching the bedding, which spread to the mosquito net. The fire blazed fiercely and became a prairie fire. Sanquan was old and frail, and his movements were slow. He could only shout for help. His son, A Yu, woke up in surprise upon hearing the sound and immediately drew water to extinguish the fire, preventing a major disaster. However, Sanquan's body had been burned by the fire and soaked in water, leading to a fire poison attacking his heart, and he died yesterday. It was a tragic event.

He Xihu, a resident of South Gate in this county, was suspected in the case of the death of a young woman, Wang Aihu, who fell into the river. He was taken into custody by the county court. Recently, the prosecutor's office investigated the case and found that Wang's death was not related to He, so he was not prosecuted. However, he was prosecuted in the criminal court for the crime of enticing a woman under the age of twenty. After repeated trials by Judge Lai, the debate concluded on the 26th of this month. He refused to accept the sentence and stated in court that he would appeal.

Building a Dam and Sluice Gate at Majishan, Changzhou 101

Majishan in District 11 of Wujin is isolated in the East Taihu Lake. During the spring and autumn seasons, the mountains are clear and the water is beautiful, and the scenery is excellent. It has always been known as a paradise. However, the farmland around the mountain along the lake, about 6,000 mu, is flooded every time the lake overflows. The mountain people watch helplessly as the torrent is unstoppable, resulting in huge losses. Qian Linshu, a member of the Rural Improvement Committee, recognizing this, invited County Magistrate Cai and others to inspect the area for a week and designed a dam and sluice gate to prevent floods. The estimated cost is about 16,000 yuan, which is difficult for the villagers to bear. Therefore, it was decided to withdraw 5,000 yuan each from the Poor Children's Home and the Relief Home, and withdraw 6,000 yuan from the public funds and public property, making a total of 16,000 yuan. The farmers along the lake wrote loan notes, specifying the repayment period. The initiators, Qian Linshu, etc., plan to start construction immediately, taking advantage of the agricultural and have sent a letter to County Magistrate Cai requesting the allocation of the funds. County Magistrate Cai transferred the letter to the Poor Children's Home, etc., on the 29th, ordering them to allocate the funds. It is expected that preparations for construction will begin soon, and the farmers in the two places are said to be delighted with this news, and the commercial cities in both places are also benefiting from this cash flow. Chenjiaba in Long Township, District 8, is a village inhabited by about 20 farm families. On the 28th of this month, Zhu Er'er's family was careless with fire after lunch, resulting in a . Robbery and Assault in Xizhang 103

Zhang Qi, a farmer in Xizhang City, District 10, is over 60 years old. He is thrifty and has accumulated some savings, which has been coveted by bandits. On the night of the 28th, more than 20 bandits suddenly came to the Zhang family, all carrying sharp knives, clubs, and flashlights. Zhang Qi woke up in alarm and was immediately seized. Zhenjiang Detective Team Cracked a Bandit Case 104

Cai Zhaofeng, captain of the detective team of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, received a confidential report that Wenmiao Town in Danyang County was robbed last month. The sixth police station of the town's public security bureau, due to its weak police force, resisted but was eventually deprived of three rifles and one Mauser pistol. It was heard that the bandits were hiding in the Cai Mao area of the provincial capital. Detectives were dispatched to investigate and obtained clues. He immediately notified the Danyang detective team to send personnel to jointly arrest them. Yesterday morning, the team cracked the case in Dantu, a county in the province, and arrested two key criminals, Feng Liangjun and Zhou Kaiju (also known as Mao Conger). They also seized a pistol, dozens of rounds of ammunition, and dozens of pieces of stolen goods such as crepe fabric. Yesterday, Yang Jinbiao, captain of the Danyang detective team, escorted them back to the county for interrogation.

Tiansunjin Silk Shop in Yangzhou Owes 50,000 Yuan 105

After the Tiansunjin Silk Shop on Yuanmen Bridge in the city went bankrupt, silk factories and trading houses from Shanghai, Hangzhou, Danyang, and Zhenjiang sent representatives to Yangzhou to negotiate the debts. The night before, together with members of the Chamber of Commerce, they sealed the shop's cabinets, but were stopped by the liquidator. It has been learned that the shop owes a total of 50,000 yuan this time. The factories and trading houses account for one-third of the total amount, and the rest are owed to local money shops and depositors. The shop's inventory is less than 10,000 yuan, so the factories and trading houses are extremely worried. They have retained a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the court and have also written to the Chamber of Commerce stating the suspicious inside story of the bankruptcy and requesting an investigation of the accounts in order to conduct a public audit. The Chamber of Commerce has forwarded the letter to the Public Security Bureau, and each has sent one police officer to guard the shop and ensure that the stored goods are not moved without authorization. Representatives of the factories and trading houses are also staying at the shop, waiting for a legal resolution.

Lawsuit Involving Aviation Lottery Tickets in Nantong 106

Yang Youheng, director of the Liuhaisha Public Security Bureau, sued Yu Chongwei, president of the Bank of China, to the Nantong County Court because the Bank of China returned a altered third-period aviation lottery ticket No. 22740, a fifth-class prize, (altered from No. 227104), denying that it was his original ticket. The prosecutor's office scheduled a preliminary hearing for the 30th. At this time, Ji Houcai, director of the Shanghai Aviation Lottery General Office, came to Tong with a photo of the entire sheet of third-period aviation lottery tickets No. 227404, a fifth-class prize, and other documents, to be presented at the court hearing.

Son of Ju Guangwen in Gaoyou Tragically Kidnapped and Murdered 107

The son of Ju Guangwen, a villager in District 5 of this county, was kidnapped by bandits a few days ago. His family reported the incident to the district regiment headquarters, which dispatched a team to arrest the bandits. This angered the bandits, and the bandits took Guangwen's son to Hebei, Wangying Town, the night before and stabbed him to death with a sharp blade. The scene was extremely tragic.

Public Sale of Anti-Japanese Goods by the Anti-Japanese Association in Jiangyin 108

The accountant, Wu Guoxiang, kept the funds and deposited them in the Bank of China. Agricultural Bank of Jiaxing Organizes Rice Mortgage 109

Wu Heshu, the manager of the bank, went to Hangzhou to contact the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank for funds, which has been settled. Warehouses have been established in Wangdian and Xin to accept rice at low interest rates. Rough rice is mortgaged at three yuan per picul. The monthly interest rate is 1.2% for cooperative members and 1.5% for non-members. Wangdian is ready and can be opened today. Xin is actively preparing and will open soon. It is learned that the farmers in the two places are delighted with this news, and the business community in both places also benefits from this cash flow. Ningbo

Local News

Successful Test Flight of China National Aviation Corporation's Southwest Route 111

Nie Kaiyi and An Lisheng Returned to Shanghai at 5 PM Yesterday

Official Opening Still Awaiting Company Meeting Decision

Guowen News Agency reports that An Lisheng, chief pilot of the China National Aviation Corporation, and Nie Kaiyi, deputy director of the aviation team, who conducted the test flight to Kunming for the purpose of opening the southwest route, returned to Shanghai at 4:40 PM yesterday. The details are recorded separately below.

Itinerary 112

Mr. An Lisheng and Mr. Nie Kaiyi, accompanied by Mr. Huang Baoxian, head of the sales team, took the company's No. 11 Sikorsky aircraft to Guangzhou on December 27th last year at around 7:00 AM. On the 31st, they encountered fog over Longzhou and were forced to land in Kao Bang, French Indochina. On January 19th of this year, they flew from Kao Bang to Kunming, and on the 26th, they flew from Kunming to Chengdu. On the 29th at 8:00 AM, they flew from Chengdu to Chongqing. At 12:45 PM that day, they took off from Chongqing and arrived in Yichang at 4:10 PM. On the 30th (yesterday) at 8:05 AM, they took off from Yichang, arrived in Hankou at 10:00 AM, took off from Hankou at 10:50 AM, arrived in Nanjing at 3:00 PM, added some engine oil, and flew to Shanghai, arriving at Longhua Airport at 4:40 PM.

Arrival in Shanghai 113

The company was informed of the arrival time of Mr. An and Mr. Nie. Important officials rushed to Longhua Airport to wait. All the staff of the aviation team stationed in Longhua also came to the airport to welcome them. After the plane landed at 4:40 PM, Mr. An and Mr. Nie got off the plane and shook hands with the welcomers one by one. Mr. Nie Kaiyi immediately telephoned Mr. Dai Enji, general manager of the company, to report that he would go to the company to report everything in person. Mr. An Lisheng, on the other hand, had been driving the plane for days and was very tired, so he briefly interacted with the welcomers and returned home to rest.

Report 114

After arriving in Shanghai, Nie Kaiyi immediately took a car to the company to report the details of the test flight and the obstruction in Vietnam to General Manager Dai Enji. Then he went to his office, briefly inspected the accumulated documents, and gave the following interview to a reporter from the Guowen News Agency.

Passing Guilin 115

Mr. Nie said that on December 31st of last year, he flew from western Guangdong and over Longzhou in Guangxi. Looking down at the airfield, there were over a thousand people doing construction work. He wanted to stop, but the airfield construction was not completed and there were many workers, making it inconvenient to land. He wanted to fly, but strange peaks rose from time to time and the weather turned worse. Moreover, he was flying west out of Pingguan and had reached the territory of French Indochina.

Obstruction in Vietnam 116

At 12:00 noon, the mountains were stacked on top of each other, the fog was thick, and the clouds were low. It was impossible to advance. He wanted to return to Longzhou, but he was afraid that there would not be enough engine oil to add. Just as he felt trapped, he suddenly found an airfield below. Although he knew it was French territory, he was forced to land. He believed that the authorities would understand. However, after landing, the local authorities in Kao Bang detained the plane. Mr. An and Mr. Nie were also hosted in separate rooms. After a week, the authorities agreed to take the train to Hanoi to negotiate the release of the plane with French Governor Daladier. Daladier said that foreign planes were absolutely not allowed to land without permission. Since they had mistakenly entered French territory, they would need a telegram from the Chinese government proving their background and requesting their release before they could comply. At this point, they began to see a glimmer of hope for the release of the plane, so they telegraphed the company. Another week passed until January 15th, when they received the French authorities' message that they would release the plane. They took a train back to Kao Bang, near Lang Son, on the 17th and arrived on the afternoon of the 18th. On the 19th, they flew to Kunming.

Climate 117

In Kao Bang, it rained lightly all day long. The ancient poem says that the land is close to the sky and it rains all year round, which is similar to what the Huayang Kingdom Chronicles says that there are no three sunny days in a row. From there, flying to Kunming, the high mountains were almost 6,200 feet above sea level. The air in Yunnan is thin. The plane descends quickly and ascends with difficulty. It took four attempts to ascend from Kunming. Therefore, this route must be flown with a large engine aircraft.

Contact 118

We stayed in Kunming for a week and were treated well by Chairman Long Yun. He also inquired in detail about the opening of the route. The Kunming authorities are eager for this route to be opened as soon as possible so that they can communicate smoothly with the central government and so that messengers can avoid the inconvenience and time-consuming detours of the Yunnan-Vietnam Railway. After contacting them, we immediately returned to Sichuan. Although the original plan was to go to Guiyang, we didn't have to go again this time because the mountains were too high and the climate was not good, and we had already conducted a test flight to Guizhou before.

Route 119

After the southwest route is opened in the future, will it go from Guangzhou or Chengdu? It will be necessary to report the test flight to the Ministry of Communications for a decision. Flying from Guangdong will have bad weather, while flying from Sichuan must pass through Zhaotong, where the mountains are 8,600 feet above sea level, making it difficult to fly.

Change of Aircraft 120

The aircraft that Mr. An and Mr. Nie took when they left was the No. 11 Sikorsky, while the one they took back to Shanghai yesterday was the No. 12 Sikorsky. It had been exchanged in Chongqing because the components of the No. 11 aircraft were more sensitive, which was more convenient for flying in the heavily mountainous area. In addition to the fact that Ms. Xia Pu, an American company employee, and Mr. Zeng Tong, a Chinese, came with Mr. An and Mr. Nie yesterday.

Li Mengbin Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 122

Wang Shouting and Lin Guogeng Went to Beijing

Chen Jiliang Will Arrive in Shanghai Within Days

Riri News Agency reports that Wang Shouting, the newly appointed Commander of the Naval Training Fleet, arrived in Shanghai to take office. Wang and Lin Jointly Go to Beijing 123

Mr. Wang first stated, "After returning to Shanghai from Xiamen, I originally intended to go to Beijing immediately to report everything to the Navy Department. However, due to handling matters related to the turnover of the training fleet, I was unable to spare the time. Now that I have taken office, things have been somewhat settled. Minister Chen (Shaokuan) telegraphed the night before last, summoning me to Beijing to discuss the deployment of coastal defense in Fujian and Xiamen in the future. It has been decided that this afternoon (the 30th) at 3:00 PM, I will leave Shanghai by train. Lin Guogeng, the Commander of Xiamen Naval Port, came to Shanghai yesterday (the 29th) to also discuss matters with the Navy Department and will be traveling with me. Li Mengbin, the Commander of Mawei Naval Port, who has been transferred to the position of Director of the Military Audit Department of the Navy Department, arrived in Shanghai this morning (the 30th) at 8:00 AM aboard the Hai Rong warship from Mawei. He originally intended to travel to Beijing together to assume his new post, but due to a cold, he plans to seek medical treatment in Shanghai and will go to Beijing after recovering in two or three days."

Recent Situation in Fujian and Xiamen 124

"After the military operations in Fuzhou, Xiamen, and other places concluded, the local area is extremely peaceful, and everything has returned to its original state. Except for the coastal defense, which is the responsibility of the Navy, the security rights of the cities of Fujian and Xiamen and all administrative agencies are ready to be handed over to the local government. In Mawei, Li Shijia is currently serving as the Commander of the Naval Port and concurrently the Brigade Commander of the First Brigade of the Marine Corps. After Li arrives in Fujian, he will be stationed in Mawei to engage in training to consolidate defense. As for the position of Provincial Government Committee Member, he will go to the province to work when necessary. In this suppression of the Fujian rebellion, in terms of rewarding meritorious service, the naval officers and soldiers absolutely dare not claim credit, because defending the country is the duty of soldiers, and it is also due to the appropriate handling by the central authorities. For two months, the Navy recovered Fujian and Xiamen without bloodshed. On the surface, it seems that not much effort was spent, but that is not the case. It is best and the highest purpose of using troops because the rebels were forced to collapse, avoiding the prolongation of war and affecting the people."

Actively Training Various Ships 125

"Now that I have taken office as the Commander of the Training Fleet, my responsibility is to train the navy and consolidate national defense. I plan to start active training from today. The ships belonging to the training fleet include the Ying Rui, Tong Ji, Jing An, and other ships. Except for the Tong Ji, which is being repaired at the Gaoyang Temple Shipyard and will be completed next month, the other ships are mostly patrolling outside. As for the torpedo team, it has been ordered to be abolished to save expenses. The ships have been separately assigned to various fleets. The Jian Kang has been assigned to the jurisdiction of the First Fleet. The Hu Peng, Hu Sun, Hu E, and Hu Ying, the four torpedo boats, have been assigned to the jurisdiction of the Second Fleet."

Chen Jiliang Will Arrive in Shanghai 126

"As for the local security and administrative responsibilities after the recovery of Fuzhou, they were temporarily the responsibility of Chen Jiliang, the Commander of the First Fleet. Now that the newly appointed Chairman of Fujian Province, Chen Yi, has arrived in Fujian, and the establishment of the provincial government is imminent, and someone is responsible for all local political affairs, it has been decided that Chen will take the Hai Chou government ship to Shanghai within days to continue his responsibilities for the defense of Songhu. After Commander Chen arrives in Shanghai, I will set out again to patrol and train the various ships. As for where to set out, it has not been ordered and is still difficult to determine."
