Rice Shops in North Shanghai Striked Yesterday 130

Workers抢Transporting Each Other in Assaults and Injuries

Rice Industry Petitions Making Demands

The Authorities Protect and Resume Business This Morning

Dagon News Agency reports that in the North Shanghai area along the Suzhou River near the New Zha Gate Bridge, the rice shops went on strike yesterday because Shi Dengfu, the foreman of the Hongtai Shoulder Transport Company, led unemployed workers to compete for work, resulting in fights. Both sides were seriously injured. After all the rice shops went on strike, they petitioned party and government agencies. The rice shops in South Shanghai also held an emergency meeting last night, preparing to take united action. The details are as follows:

Gathering Crowds for抢Transporting 131

Shi Dengfu, the foreman of the Hongtai Yuji Shoulder Transport Company, led unemployed workers in December last year to搶shoulder transport work from the shoulder carriers and handcart drivers of the rice shops, which led to disputes. After the Social Affairs Bureau, together with the City Party Department and the Public Security Bureau, conducted mediation and decided on four solutions, the matter came to an end. At 8:00 AM the day before yesterday, the foreman Shi Dengfu again led more than 200 unemployed workers to gather at the Suzhou River Rice Industry Wharf, claiming that according to the mediation record of the Social Affairs Bureau, they wanted to be安置. The order was disrupted at the time. The rice shops, fearing that unfortunate incidents would occur, notified the rice boats to announce the suspension of unloading. Unexpectedly, at 9:00 AM yesterday morning, more than 100 unemployed workers gathered again, wearing red-edged blue vests, and rushed forward to搶work while the shoulder carriers were unloading.

Fights Occurred 132

Seeing the unemployed workers coming aggressively, the shoulder carriers and handcart drivers of the rice shops announced the suspension of unloading. More and more workers gathered on both sides, and the confrontational situation was extremely serious. At that time, the unemployed workers first started arguing. After a disagreement, they resorted to violence. The order was chaotic for a while. Both sides fought each other with carrying poles and shoulder poles. Pedestrians and vehicles dodged to both sides, causing traffic to be cut off in the area of the New Zha Gate Bridge and Datong Road.

Injury Investigation 133

During the fighting, quite a few unemployed workers were injured. It is learned that the names of the injured include Li Tianhao, Chen Fuyuan, Jiang Xiubo, Chen Dayuan, Sun Shangkui, and others. All of their heads were seriously injured. Jiang Changkun, Yi Jinsong, Sun Yazi, Liu Xiaozhi, Sun Chuanxing, Jiang Tianming, and others also suffered injuries to their feet and waists. However, Leng Shanlin and Xu Songlin were the most seriously injured, and there was fear for their lives. The Fourth District Public Security Bureau dispatched police to transport all the injured to the Second Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society on Carter Road for treatment. Leng Shanlin and Xu Songlin were hospitalized for treatment due to their serious injuries. The other workers were bandaged by doctors and discharged from the hospital immediately. After being interrogated by the Fourth District Public Security Bureau, they were sent to the local court for examination of injuries.

Military Police Suppression 134

After hearing the news, Lai Gang, the director of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau, immediately led more than 30 police officers to suppress the violence, but the number of people was too large to control. He immediately telegraphed Wu, the captain of the Second Squadron of the Security Brigade, to dispatch a team to suppress the violence together. After learning about this, Wen Hongen, the director of the City Public Security Bureau, also ordered the police brigade to dispatch more than 20 police officers to ride in a security vehicle to the area to distribute and strictly guard the area. It was not until after 11:00 AM that the workers on both sides were dispersed separately.

Detain and Interrogate 135

After the shoulder carriers and handcart drivers caused the above disturbances, the Fourth District Public Security Bureau dispatched police to arrest Yi Guocai, a handcart driver, and Zhang Caiyuan, Chen Fuyuan, Li Tianhao, Jiang Changkun, Li Zhengbang, Xu Zhonglin, Liu Xueren, Xue Deshi, Li Jinsong, Chen Dayuan, Sun Chengkui, Xiao San, Wang Guangfu, Leng Hai, Jiang Xiubo, Shen Fugao, Deng Zhikuan, and 18 others, including a mute. More than a dozen of them were slightly or seriously injured, and two iron bars, two iron hooks, and two bamboo boards were found. According to the statements of the handcart drivers and shoulder carriers, each made excuses. They were ordered to be escorted to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. It was also heard that there were still several people who were more seriously injured, and the fire brigade dispatched ambulances to send them to the hospital for treatment. Afterward, Director Wen Hongen immediately issued a hand order to investigate and arrest Gao Qifeng, the head of the rice merchants in Zhabei, who started the incident. Director Lai dispatched Officer Mu to lead the police to arrest Gao. According to his confession,

He is 38 years old and from Gaoyou. He refused to confess to the fighting between the handcart drivers and the shoulder carriers. It is now known that the Zhabei Rice Grain Association and various rice shops have dispatched a security team to protect them.

Financial Strike 136

The rice shops and manufacturers from the north end of the New Zha Gate Bridge to Wuzhen Road on Guangfu Road were indignant at this situation and announced a general strike at noon to await the resolution of the party and government agencies. The Dagon News Agency reporter went to the area to investigate separately. The closed shops included Wanshengtai, Yutai Xing, Fengtai, Changfeng, Yiqingshun, Yidachang, Runyu, Dade, Damao, Hengkang, Zhicheng, Tongxinggong, Wanyuanhe, Daxin, Rentai, Yuanfeng, Juxingsheng, Yongshuntai, Xiechangde, Defeng, Yuchangxiang, Ruichangfa, Yisheng, Yusheng, Dayouheng, Hefengtai, Hongchang, and more than 30 others. The signboards were also all tightly closed. Yesterday, more than 30 rice boats arriving at the Suzhou River also completely suspended unloading.

Emergency Meeting 137

After all the rice industry firms and factories went on strike, an emergency meeting was held at 2:00 PM at the Doumi Guild Hall on Kulun Road in Zhabei to discuss countermeasures. More than 50 representatives of the rice industry firms and factories, including Jiang Shizhi and Fu Qiangen, were present. Lu Jingwen was elected as the chairman to report that the unemployed workers had repeatedly harassed them and that the rice merchants had painfully suspended business. It was decided to take the following measures: (1) According to the last joint meeting resolution, all business will be suspended to await resolution. (2) Lu Jingwen and Jiang Shizhi were elected as representatives to petition party and government agencies to demand a cessation of the disturbances in order to maintain business. (3) If there is no effective solution, the market will not be opened. (4) A letter will be sent to the rice merchants in South Shanghai to express unanimous agreement.

Petitioning the Authorities 138

The rice industry firms and factories, because Shi Dengfu repeatedly interfered with business, the conference elected representatives Jiang Shizhi, Lu Jingwen, and others to petition the Social Affairs Bureau in the city center at 3:00 PM. Wang Xianqing, the mediation director of the Third Section, received them. The rice industry representatives reported the situation of the disturbances and immediately presented five demands: (1) Before the case is resolved, all workers in Shi Dengfu's group wearing numbered uniforms must not go to the Wusong River Rice Industry Wharf again. (2) If Shi Dengfu's group of workers goes to the Rice Industry Wharf again, the police must arrest them immediately. (3) Shi Dengfu's license should be revoked immediately. (4) All firms and factories are unwilling to do business until they receive effective guarantees. (5) If the North Shanghai issue cannot be resolved tomorrow, the South Shanghai side will also follow suit. Mr. Wang persuaded the rice merchants to open the market first. The Social Affairs Bureau will transfer the matter to the Public Security Bureau and send police to protect them. All other issues will be resolved appropriately in the near future. The representatives returned until after 5:00 PM.

Business Resumes Today 139

After all the rice industry firms and factories went on strike yesterday, the matter was very important for the people's livelihood. The Social Affairs Bureau is responsible for protection, and police have been dispatched to maintain order. It has been decided to open the market at 8:00 AM this morning. Other issues will be resolved by the authorities.

Mr. Wang Shengsan, an Elder, is Scheduled to Open His Funeral

Mr. Wang Shengsan, a respected elder in Shanghai, whose taboo name was Fenggao, was from the Fahua Town of Shanghai. He studied at the Tongwen Guan in his youth and was a pioneer in the study of European languages by Chinese people. In the fifteenth year of Guangxu, he followed Xue Taichang Fucheng of Wuxi on a mission to the four countries of England, France, Italy, and Belgium, providing much assistance. He then requested leave to return to China in the twenty-first year of Guangxu. At that time, Sheng Gongbao Yihuai of Wujin was revitalizing industry. Hearing of Mr. Wang's talent, he was appointed to assist in the exploration of coal and iron mines. In the twenty-seventh year of Guangxu, Scholar Cai Jun was ordered to serve as ambassador to Japan and奏appointed Mr. Wang as参赞. Later, he was reassigned as the Consul General in Yokohama. In the twenty-eighth year of Guangxu, he returned to China to take the examination and was awarded the eighteenth place舉人. After the庚子Rebellion, the Qing court tried hard to innovate, and an edict was issued to派戴尚书Hongci and Duan Zhijun Fang to serve as ambassadors to Europe and the United States to investigate politics. Mr. Wang was appointed as参赞. Wherever the official car went, he was given实星 by the governments of Germany, France, Russia, Italy, Belgium, and Austria. After returning to China in the thirty-second year of Guangxu, he was soon awarded the second-rank顶戴浙江 candidate道because of his labor. In Zhejiang, he successively served as the head of the Provincial Police Bureau, the head of the Provincial Anti-Smoking Bureau, the head of the Telephone Bureau, and the head of the Provincial Foreign Affairs Bureau and the Bureau of Agriculture, Industry, Commerce, and Mines. He founded a new government, not avoiding labor and resentment. He was granted the title of Zhejiang 交涉使 in the second year of Xuantong. He successively ordered the Japanese merchants in Hangzhou and Jiangshan to move and close, and recovered the Baoshi Mountain in West Lake, the Yanji Mountain in Gongchen Bridge, the Haidao in Huzhou, and the Yin Mountain in Taizhou. His deeds were recorded and praised. After the鼎革, in the seventh year of the Republic of China, he was reappointed as Zhejiang Special 交涉员 for seven years. He was awarded the second-class 大綬嘉禾章 for his labor. In the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, after the May 30th Massacre occurred, the students of St. John's University in Shanghai clashed with the president and the entire school withdrew. Mr. Wang, old but strong, saw righteousness and acted bravely. He donated 100 acres of his ancestors' cemetery to found Guanghua University. The school, now standing on the Daxi Road in West Shanghai, is the crystallization of Mr. Wang's efforts. When the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army arrived in Shanghai, Mr. Wang, with his high age and great reputation, was pushed to act as the Director of the Songhu Commercial Port. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, he was appointed as the Director of the Hubei Provincial Parcel Tax Bureau. He suffered a stroke in the autumn of the following year and returned to Shanghai to recuperate. He eventually passed away on the 23rd day of November last winter due to his declining physical strength, at the age of seventy-six. He had four sons. Looking at Mr. Wang's life, he served the country and society, and his career was remarkable. He can be passed down in history. Moreover, he was generous and righteous, and treated people with sincerity. Those who knew him all respected and loved him. He was not only known for his diplomatic progress. It is now heard that Mr. Wang's family has chosen February 1st to open the funeral at the Hushe at the intersection of Beijing Road and Guizhou Road, and February 2nd at the Buddhist Jingye Society at 480 Hard Road. Mr. Wang has acquaintances all over Shanghai, and it is expected that there will be a grand scene of plain cars and white horses at that time.

City Chamber of Commerce Telegram Request

Striving for a Reduction in German Egg Tax 143

Should be in Accordance with the Principle of Equality and Mutual Benefit

Please Order the German Ambassador to Pay Attention When Concluding the Treaty

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing yesterday, "[To the] Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Nanjing, On the 28th of this month, we received a letter from the Egg Industry Association, stating that, according to the Havas News Agency report on January 24th, the Sino-German Commercial Treaty has expired, and the Chinese ambassador to Germany is conducting a renewal in Berlin. Upon investigation, in recent years, our country's exports of eggs and egg products have plummeted. Just taking exports to Germany as an example, in 1932, the German government increased the import tax on Chinese frozen eggs to 65 marks per 100 kilograms, which is 650 marks per ton (1,000 kilograms). The tax on fresh eggs was increased to 70 marks per 100 kilograms. This heavy tax far exceeds the cost of Chinese eggs arriving in Germany, which is tantamount to prohibiting the import of our country's eggs and eggs. Therefore, the trade of Chinese eggs to Germany is almost completely cut off. (According to recent customs records, there has been an increase in Chinese eggs transported to Germany, but in fact, the number of eggs sold directly to Germany is very small. Most of the Chinese eggs are first transported to the Hamburg docks. Hamburg is a free port, and goods only go to the docks without going through customs. Sales to Germany do not incur taxes. After Chinese eggs go to the docks, they are transported to nearby countries depending on the needs.) The German government offers special preferential treatment for taxes levied on eggs and egg products transported to German customs from other countries. For example, Chinese fresh eggs are taxed at 70 marks per 100 kilograms, while those transported from the Netherlands or other countries are only taxed at 30 marks per 100 kilograms. This unequal treatment violates the principle of mutual trade benefits. It has also been found that in the past three years, China-Germany trade has been completely in deficit in our country, and Germany has always been in a favorable position. German goods exported to China are always three times more than Chinese goods exported to Germany. A comparative table of China-Germany trade from 1930 to 1932 is as follows: (The figures on the left are in customs silver)

Year German Goods Exported to China Chinese Goods Exported to Germany Our Country's Deficit

1930 69,000,000 taels 23,360,000 45,640,000

1931 83,500,000 23,138,000 60,362,000

1932 71,800,000 29,824,000 41,976,000

Looking at the table on the right, German goods flooded into China in the past three years, with a total deficit of about 147 million taels. The export of Chinese goods to Germany is getting worse. Looking at our country's rural economy, it has been extremely depressed, and the farmers in the 18 provinces of the ministry who rely on eggs as a side product for their livelihoods are countless. Since the foreign trade of eggs and egg products has been subject to various blows, the farmers have fallen into even greater distress. If we want to revive the countryside, there are many ways to do it, but restoring the foreign trade of eggs and egg products is an urgent measure. For this reason, we urgently sent this letter to your association, imploring you to quickly电通知 our country's ambassador to Germany to do its utmost to protect our country's trade in eggs to Germany in accordance with the principle of equality and mutual benefit when renewing the Sino-German Commercial Treaty. Considering the past comparison of trade between the two countries, Germany is already in a favorable position, and the German government should improve the treatment of Chinese egg imports. Even if it cannot offer special preferential treatment, it should at least treat the import of eggs from other countries to Germany in the same way, which is reasonable. It has been found that Article 1, paragraph 2 of the new agreement on tariff issues signed between China and Germany in the 17th year of the Republic of China states that one of the contracting states, under any circumstances, may not levy higher or different taxes, internal taxes, or any donations on the goods transported and exported by the people of the other country within its territory than those paid by its own people or the people of any other country. According to this agreement, the taxes levied by Germans on Chinese eggs transported to Germany must not be higher or different than those of other countries. We request that your ministry电notify the embassy in Germany, ordering it to strive for this and pay attention when revising the new treaty, which is a public matter. Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce叩艶."

National Production Conference

Exchanged Views with Industrial Department Yesterday 144

Preparatory Committee Hosted Banquet for Director of Industry Department Liu Yin Fu

New Voice News Agency reports that the National Production Conference, after the appointment of the preparatory committee, yesterday afternoon at 7:00 PM, specially hosted a banquet for Liu Yinfu, the director of the Industrial Department of the Ministry of Industry, at the Yiyou Club on Hankou Road, and exchanged views. The following is a record of Director Liu's speech:

Hosting Banquet for Mr. Liu 145

The preparatory committee and conveners of the National Production Conference hosted a banquet for Liu Yinfu, the director of the Industrial Department of the Ministry of Industry, at the Yiyou Club on Hankou Road yesterday at 7:00 PM, and held a conversation meeting during the banquet. The attendees included Guo Shun, Wang Yunwu, Wu Yun Chu, Qian Chengxu, Hu Xiyuan, Mu Ouchu, Rong Zongjing, and Director Liu, totaling more than 20 people. It is heard that as a result of the exchange of views, regarding (1) the scope of the proposals and the conference expenses, considerable decisions have been made in principle.

Director Liu Speaks 146

Director Liu told a reporter from the New Sound Society that the convocation of this production conference was originally based on proposals from Central Committee members such as Sun Zhesheng and Wu Chaoshu during the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee, in order to save our country's declining production crisis. The list of conveners for each province and city was determined entirely according to the state of industrial development in each province and city, with more from those that are more developed and fewer from those that are less developed. Those invited are all respected figures in the industrial sector. It is hoped that this conference will pay more attention to the environment and factual aspects, avoid empty talk and useless general proposals, and hope that it will be easier to promote and implement in the future. In my opinion, the general key points of the scope of discussion for this conference can be divided into two categories: (A) Regarding economic aspects, such as (1) how to invite the financial sector to invest in domestic production enterprises, (2) implementing tariff protection policies and reducing tax rates on produced goods, and (3) transportation issues related to transportation; (B) Regarding the manufacturers themselves, such as (1) improvements in management systems related to organizational aspects, reforms in accounting systems, and improvements in sales methods, (2) product improvements related to technical aspects, and (3) how to develop domestic raw materials. The reason why our country has actually declined in recent years and has not been able to make significant progress is partly due to various political factors, and partly due to the failure of manufacturers themselves to have sound organization, which is also a major reason. Observing the development of foreign industries in China, although there are differences in circumstances, in terms of all organization and technology, they are superior to us. Therefore, whatever the outcome of this conference, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce generally hopes that manufacturers can devote themselves to this.

Ammonium Sulfate Plant 147

He continued, saying that the Industrial Department of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is now doing its best to stand in a promoting position to advance various industries. Since the January 28th Incident, it has deeply felt the lack of raw materials in industry, especially during the intense Shanghai battle, the principle of ammonium sulfate, a major item, encountered great difficulties. If a remedy is not sought quickly, it will be related to national defense, which is no small matter. Therefore, in view of this, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce immediately began preparing to establish its own ammonium sulfate plant. Since the start of the project, many foreign merchants have been willing to invest. After deliberation, it was decided that it would be run purely by domestic commercial shares, with a total capital of 10 million yuan. The investors are all from the financial and industrial sectors. Recently, the Central Political Conference decided to establish it within one year, so it is expected that it will be gradually realized soon.

Establishing an Alcohol Plant 148

He also said that since the Ministry of Industry and Commerce took the initiative to set up an alcohol plant, many people in Shanghai and other parts of the country have been willing to open one. However, in order to take into account the actual needs of the country, one plant will still be jointly operated by government and business, with exclusive operation. For the time being, no other alcohol plants will be allowed to be established in the areas of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Fujian provinces, so as to avoid the historical senseless competition of Chinese merchants, resulting in the disadvantage of oversupply. However, in the future, if the need arises and the supply is insufficient, temporary flexible measures can also be taken. Since preparations began, the date of establishment is not far off.

Central Machine Factory 149

As for the Central Machine Factory, since it was decided to proceed with the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity funds, in the future, the procurement of materials for machinery will be handled by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Purchasing Committee. Preparations have been completed. Although the factory site was previously selected in the city of Nanjing, one reason is that the terrain needs to be higher, and the second is to consider the convenience of purchasers, so it is still under study. Once the factory site is determined, the construction funds are raised, and the machinery is ready, it only needs to be formally notified and can be transported within three months. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce also hopes to realize it within this year. As for the steel plant issue, it is of great importance and requires careful study. It is too early to say when it will be signed.

Factory Inspection 150

Finally, it was also stated in response that the issue of factory inspection in the Shanghai Municipal Council concession had been progressing very smoothly on both sides. However, due to the issue of jurisdiction on the concession side, obstacles occurred, delaying it to this day. However, because this matter falls within the scope of the Labor Department, I am not very familiar with it. However, I understand that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is determined to promote this measure because it concerns the welfare and safety of workers, and will soon renegotiate a compromise with the Shanghai concession authorities.

Continued News on the Interruption of Navigation in Madang due to Shallow Water

Difficulty in Rescuing Stranded Vessels

Unpredictable Changes in Lao Xingang

The shallow water and interrupted navigation on the Yangtze River have been reported in yesterday's newspaper. The following is a continuation of the news:

Jianguo Escapes Danger and Returns to Shanghai 154

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River vessel Jianguo was delayed due to being blocked by shallow water in Madang. It was only after the Anqing branch sent a ship to tow it that the Jianguo was pulled away from the shoal. It did not enter the port until yesterday afternoon, arriving more than thirty hours late. After unloading the cargo today, the ship will enter the factory for repairs. The Sanbei Songpu vessel was also blocked in Madang. It later went to Jiujiang, unloaded cargo, and reduced the load before setting sail. It did not arrive until yesterday afternoon.

Four Ships Rescue Changxing 155

The Sanbei Company's Changxing vessel has been stranded in Madang for three days. It was not until yesterday that the Sanbei vessel was sent to tow it, but to no avail. Later, Hankou also sent the shallow water Yongkang vessel to tow it, but it still could not be towed away from the shoal. Now, the Sanbei vessel is being used to unload its cargo. The bureau has also transferred the Fuyang vessel to unload and tow. As the passengers on the ship have been delayed for many days, the Jing'an vessel was ordered to transfer them. The passengers will go to Hankou first, while rescue efforts continue.

Madang Water Gauge Report 156

It is found that the shallowest point in Madang is 45 and a half miles upstream of Anqing, 7 and a half miles from Xiaogushan, and 45 miles from Jiujiang upstream. There was originally an old channel there. A new port was opened last year, which could be two hours faster. The old port is arc-shaped and the new port is straight. Now the new port water is shallower and ships are prohibited from going up and down. The old port is still used. Yesterday's water gauge report stated that the water had dropped to only 9 feet 1 inch. The second telegram said that it was 9 feet 3 inches, but it was still impossible to navigate.

All Four Hong Vessels Blocked 157

The Sanbei Company's upper river shallow water vessels Hongyuan, Hongzhen, Hongli, and Hongheng are all blocked due to the Yangtze River's shallow water. These four vessels are more suitable for sailing downstream. Unexpectedly, in the Xindi area, because they were carrying salt into Hunan, they were all blocked and none could sail downstream. Yesterday, China Merchants' Jianghua vessel still set sail, but only went to Anqing, using barges to transport cargo. Jianghua sailed empty upstream to load cargo to Hankou.

Shanghai Municipal Council

Annual Report of the Prison Director 159

The Shanghai Municipal Council Police Department Extra-Department Chief and Prison Management Department Chief's work report for the previous year stated that at the beginning of the year, there were 6,662 prisoners in the Ward Road Prison, and at the end of the year there were 6,312. The highest number was on June 15, with 6,757. The average number each year for the past ten years is:

1924: 1,800 prisoners. 1925: 2,116 prisoners. 1926: 2,231 prisoners. 1927: 2,457 prisoners. 1928: 3,460 prisoners. 1929: 4,422 prisoners. 1930: 5,067 prisoners. 1931: 6,300 prisoners. 1932: 6,695 prisoners. 1933: 6,563 prisoners.

At the end of the year, the sentences of the 6,312 prisoners were: 75 life imprisonment, 229 imprisonment for more than 15 years, 397 imprisonment for more than 10 years, 678 imprisonment for more than 7 years, 473 imprisonment for more than 5 years, 746 imprisonment for more than 3 years, 786 imprisonment for more than 2 years, 1,367 imprisonment for more than 1 year, 781 imprisonment for more than 6 months, 336 imprisonment for more than 3 months, 219 imprisonment for more than 1 month, 196 imprisonment for more than 2 days, 21 sentenced to death, and 8 temporarily detained awaiting trial.

According to the National Government's amnesty regulations, 581 people were released successively within this year after their sentences were reduced. In total, including the prisoners released under this item in the previous year, there were 2,564. Among them, 706 were arrested again for other cases and sentenced to imprisonment again.

The health and behavior of the prisoners this year were generally good. There were 194 deaths due to illness (232 in the previous year) and 6 suicides. One person was transferred to the new prison hospital for treatment due to pathological reasons. The new prison hospital started working on November 20, with an average of 746 outpatient visits per day and 222 inpatients.

After the establishment of the new reformatory, qualified teachers were able to take charge of the intellectual, physical, and vocational training of juvenile offenders. This year, 58 juvenile offenders were transferred from the court. Their general behavior and health were good.

The Western Prison on Xiamen Road received 60 male prisoners from the Consular Court, 239 from the Local Court, 1 female prisoner from the Consular Court, 67 from the Local Court, and 3 male juvenile offenders, all from the Local Court. In addition, there were 111 prisoners temporarily detained in two categories. As of the end of the year, there were 62 male prisoners and 5 female prisoners in prison. Fourteen prisoners were released after serving their sentences, and were given assistance by the Released Prisoners Relief Association. The conditions of the prisoners on Xiamen Road were also good. This year, 9 people were released under the amnesty law. Three people were arrested and sentenced again after being released.

On average, among the 2,080 people who were able to work in prisoner handicrafts, 1,597 worked every day, which is 67 percent. The items produced included sandbags, hemp blankets, uniforms, boots, rickshaw donation plates, woodenware, rattan ware, etc. In addition, they also performed repair work for the Public Works Department, as well as printing documents and binding books for the Municipal Council. The new workshop was completed in November, so more prisoners were able to work.

The City Standard Clock

Reasons for Stopping or Being Inaccurate 160

The City Public Works Bureau is Changing the Lines

Since the establishment of electric standard clocks in Shanghai South and Zhabei, the citizens have found them very convenient. However, recently, these standard clocks have sometimes stopped or been inaccurate, which is a bit of a drawback. According to inquiries by reporters to the City Public Works Bureau, when these standard clocks were first set up,

due to a lack of funds, all the lines used bare copper wires temporarily borrowed from telephone poles. As a result, whenever there were strong winds and rain or telephone workers repaired telephone lines, the lines were inevitably touched, causing the standard clocks to stop or have differences in speed. The bureau is now trying to change the standard clock lines and will eliminate this problem in the shortest possible time.

Young Resident of Henan Hostel Commits Suicide by Taking Poison 162

On the evening before last at around 7:00 p.m., a young man named Zhou Zhifang, aged about 20, arrived at the Henan Hostel at No. 3, Lane 426, North Henan Road. He booked room number 12. At around 10:00 a.m. the next morning, the hostel tea servant Jiang Qingxi discovered a sobbing sound in the room, which aroused his suspicion. He immediately opened the door and entered, and saw him lying on the bed, his face pale. He also saw an opium box on the table, and knew that he had taken poison. He immediately reported to the Hongkou Police Station, and ordered detectives to go to investigate. They immediately took him to Tongren Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective and he soon died. The body was taken to the Forensic Examination Office on Filun Road. Detectives found a suicide note beside the deceased, addressed to his parents, which stated that he was suffering from economic difficulties, which led to the thought of ending his life, etc. However, there was no address on the letter, so it was impossible to deliver it. A wallet was also found, containing only four small dollars and four pawn tickets, as well as a card printed with the words "Xue Guanxing." The detectives then knew that Zhou Zhifang was an alias. At 10:00 a.m. yesterday morning, Prosecutor Diao Chengtang was dispatched by the First Special District Local Court to examine the body. According to Jiang Qingxi's report of the previous situation:

Prosecutor Diao concluded that the deceased, Xue Guanxing, male, indeed died from taking opium poison during his lifetime. The body was handed over to Pushan Villa for burial.

Shi Guiyang Commits Suicide by Taking Poison After Embezzling Funds 163

Heavy Smoker, Life in Danger

Yesterday afternoon, a traveler entered the Rongtai Hotel at No. 516 Hua Fa Mingguo Road. The tea boy led him to room 21. He claimed to be Shi Guiyang, 20 years old, from Nanjing, and worked at the World Book Company on Fourth Horse Road. His family lived at No. 1 Xianqing Lane, Laoximen. Recently, due to excessive extravagance, he embezzled more than 300 yuan of his brother's (who opened a bookstore) book accounts and squandered them. However, when the end of the lunar year arrived, his brother discovered it and strictly investigated. Guiyang had no way to turn things around and was at a loss. Therefore, he had no face to see his father and brothers at home, so he temporarily took refuge in an inn, swallowed a large amount of raw opium, and committed suicide behind people's backs. Fortunately, the tea boy discovered it early, and immediately called his father, Gengsheng (at Hua Fang Photo Studio in Ximen), to the scene to help transport him to Renji Hospital. However, the rescue was ineffective, and he died at midnight at 12.

Red Pills Seized and Bribed Release 164

Yan Chuntang, a well-known seller of red pills in this port, has a factory in Shanghai that manufactures poisonous pills with the trademark "Golden Rooster." He sends partners to Changzhou, Wuxi, Jiangyin, and other areas to sell them, and the sales are quite wide. A few days ago, Inspector Jiang of the Pengjian Town branch of the Kunshan County Public Security Bureau intercepted a transport ship in the river at Datong Bridge and seized more than 1,200 catties of Golden Rooster brand red pills, as well as the ship's partners. They learned that they were sold by Yan Chuntang and were being transported to Wuxi for sale. When Yan learned in Shanghai that the red pill ship had been detained, he sent someone to Kunshan overnight to ask the local gangster leader to intercede with Inspector Jiang. As a result, Yan paid 1,300 yuan to redeem the transport ship and the red pills it contained, which continued to sail to Wuxi for sale. After learning about this from a visit by Hua Shijun, the Director of the County Public Security Bureau, in addition to widely dispatching detectives to strictly block the various key areas, he also sent a detective team leader to Shanghai a few days ago to conduct a secret investigation. Yesterday, he took a car back to Kunshan, reported the findings of the investigation to Director Hua, and prepared a document to come to Shanghai to transfer the leader Yan Chuntang back to the case for interrogation in order to suppress the toxic atmosphere.

Fan Aisheng Case

Kidnappers Interrogated Yesterday Morning 165

One Kidnapper Used to be an Elementary School Principal

All Criminals Detained and Investigation Continues

Fan Aisheng, a native of Jiangyin, lives at No. 31 Guluo Road in the French Concession. He opened the Dehe Gongqing Company on Ningbo Road. At 7:30 p.m. on the 23rd of last month, Fan took his private car from the company to return home. When passing Guangxi Road near Shantou Road, he was suddenly kidnapped by kidnappers and extorted a huge sum of money. Until yesterday, Chinese Chief Detective You A'gen of the Old Gate Police Station received a report that the kidnappers had contacted Fan's family, at 6:00 p.m., at the intersection of Gansi East Road and West Aishi Road in the French Concession,

To Discuss Ransom 166

Matters, he immediately ordered Chinese detectives Zhou Guisen, Zhang Yuanqing, Liu Junqing, Xie Shuiquan, and others to disguise themselves separately and ambush in the vicinity. He also ordered Chinese detective Shen Jinwen to impersonate a representative of Fan's family, holding a piece of preserved meat in one hand and a letter from the kidnappers in the other. Chinese detectives Liu Ziliang, Yan Shiqing, and Bao Detective Wang Yifei hid in a nearby house, ready to act as needed. After the deployment was completed, they set off separately. When Detective Shen arrived at the scene, he saw a person riding a bicycle passing in front of Shen, blowing a whistle in his mouth, and told him to follow him west. Shen ignored him. Then the person came again and told Shen to go south. Shen ignored him again. Before long, another man

Holding a Handgun 167

Approached Detective Shen and pointed a gun at him, telling him to follow him. Shen followed him step by step. At that time, detective Liu Ziliang suddenly stepped forward from behind and hugged the bandit's waist. Unexpectedly, the bandit immediately fired a shot at Liu with the gun, hitting his shoulder. The ambushing detectives, seeing the emergency, rushed forward and captured the bandit, snatching a handgun with four bullets inside, and nine bullets were found on his body. He was interrogated and learned that his name was Liu Ziyu, from Shandong. He also confessed that the hostage was hidden at No. 10 Shunan Lane, West Aishi Road. The detectives immediately went there, but

No One Was There 168

They rescued the hostage Fan Aisheng in the pavilion room on the third floor. After searching, they also seized 20 bullets, two house rental receipt stamps, and 85 yuan. Then another person from Jiangbei, Qiu Yulou, was found on the drying platform. After a while, Cui Yaowen (also known as Zi

Ming), a native of Chongming, was found wandering in the lane. His behavior was suspicious and he was caught by the detectives. They were all taken to the police station. It was found that the house where the hostage was hidden was rented by Cui under the alias Li Jinming from the owner. Qiu Yulou also confessed that he was hired by Cui as a servant. The house was also rented by Cui. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Criminal Division of the First Special Court, where Criminal Judge Qian Hongye interrogated them. Police lawyer Li Zhishan stated the above situation, and said that this case

The remaining accomplices are being arrested, so please reschedule the hearing. Liu also instructed me to write a letter. I told him that I had no property. He said that two relatives, Wu Tongwen, had forced me to write a letter home. Under Jin's Instruction 170

Imported Bicycles

Japanese Goods Overwhelm British Goods 171

Chinese Merchants Have Forgotten the National Crisis

The Japanese Newspaper Naturally Praises It

According to yesterday's Japanese-language Shanghai Japanese Newspaper, the popularity of bicycles in China has recently surged. Shanghai, being the foremost commercial and industrial city in China, is witnessing a scramble for bicycles for transporting goods. The reasons for the prevalence of bicycles are threefold: firstly, the speed of bicycles has increased, making them suitable for commercial warfare; secondly, they save labor; thirdly, they eliminate the worry of theft; and fourthly, they are convenient to use. This is a sign of cultural progress among Chinese merchants. Currently, most of the bicycles used are from Japan. Last year's import volume was approximately 570,000 yuan, of which 290,000 yuan came from Japan and 200,000 yuan from Britain. If calculated separately for the months around October last year, July saw 70,000 yuan, with Japan accounting for 31,000 yuan and Britain 30,000 yuan; August saw 45,000 yuan, with Japan 17,000 yuan and Britain 18,000 yuan, and Germany 10,000 yuan; September saw 51,000 yuan, with Japan 18,000 yuan and Britain 24,000 yuan; October saw 58,000 yuan, with Japan 38,000 yuan and Britain 14,000 yuan; November saw 47,000 yuan, with Japan 25,000 yuan and Britain 13,000 yuan; December saw 40,000 yuan, with Japan 23,000 yuan and Britain 12,000 yuan. From the above, it can be seen that Japanese products have overwhelmed British products. The quantity of imported bicycle accessories has also increased accordingly.

The Xinningxing Encountered a Severe Storm

A Wave Pushed it Back 20 Li 172

It Returned Safely to Shanghai Yesterday

The Xinningxing vessel of the Sanbei Company, on its voyage from Xiamen to Shanghai this time, encountered a severe storm en route. The ship's hull was in extreme danger and nearly capsized. Fortunately, the vessel escaped danger and arrived in Shanghai yesterday. It is indeed fortunate. It is noted that the Xinningxing vessel was previously dispatched to Fujian and then to Xiamen. On the 25th, the ship departed from Xiamen, heading back to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, when sailing in the open sea off Xiamen, between 118 degrees 34 minutes East longitude and 24 degrees 13 minutes North latitude, it encountered a severe storm. At that time, around 11 a.m., the captain of the Xinningxing, realizing that a storm had suddenly arisen on the sea and that the ship had no way to avoid it, urgently directed the ship to sail against the wind to avoid a major disaster. However, the wind and waves were too strong. The Xinningxing, running at full speed, could not withstand the onslaught of the storm. A wave surged, and the water even went over the ship's hull. The spray reached the bridge, causing seawater to enter various parts of the ship. At the most critical moment, the ship's hull was even tilted sideways by the huge waves, nearly capsizing. All the crew members and sailors engaged in rescue work, fighting against the fierce wind and waves. The situation was even more perilous at night. At that time, radio communication was also impossible. From noon on the 25th to noon on the 26th, after 24 hours of storm attack, the crew members, working tirelessly amidst the raging waves, without food or sleep, worked together to save the ship. Normally, at least 240 to 250 nautical miles could be traveled in 24 hours, but on that day, only 30 nautical miles were covered in the severe storm, which proves the strength of the wind and the ferocity of the waves. By noon on the 26th, the wind was even stronger, and the waves were even bigger. The Xinningxing was in extreme danger, but it was pushed back 20 nautical miles by the strong wind before finally reaching Huitan Bay. The ship's hull turned from danger to safety. At this time, the captain ordered the ship to anchor there temporarily to avoid the wind and sent a telegram to Shanghai, briefly stating that the Xinningxing had encountered a storm, and the ship's hull was about to capsize. From noon yesterday to noon today, only 30 li had been traveled, but it had been pushed back 20 li by the wind. The situation was extremely dangerous. It was now sheltering from the storm in Huitan Bay and reorganizing the ship's body. After the wind subsided slightly, the ship was able to weigh anchor and head to Shanghai. It was originally planned to dock in Min, but due to the delay caused by the wind and waves, the voyage was delayed. Therefore, it sailed directly to Shanghai. It arrived safely in Shanghai yesterday. The ship is now docked in Pudong. Afterwards, the crew members spoke of the dangers of the great storm and turned pale at the mention of it. However, they returned safely to Shanghai, and the crew members were unharmed, and the hull was also as good as new. It was indeed fortunate. Now, the ship is still planning to be dispatched to Fuzhou in a day or two.

Tai Hengyuan Gold Shop

Robbed in the Early Morning 173

Losses Amounted to 10,000 Yuan

Tai Hengyuan Gold Shop, located at No. 15 Qingyuan Road, Beijing Road, specializes in gold trading. Unexpectedly, at around 10 a.m. yesterday morning, while the shop assistants were sorting out market information, six robbers suddenly broke into the shop. They spoke in Northern and local accents and wore long and short gowns of varying colors. Each carried a handgun. Two of the robbers first guarded the front and back doors separately, while the remaining robbers shouted at the shopkeeper and assistants in the store, ordering them to be silent and confining them to a room. After forcing the accountant to hand over the key to the safe, they carried out the confinement. The robbers then looted wantonly, taking all the silver dollars and cash. The total loss amounted to more than 10,000 yuan. After the robbers left, the shop assistants were able to regain their freedom. However, they saw that the store was in a chaotic state and could not be inventoried. They urgently telegraphed the Central Police Station to report the incident. The police station dispatched a large number of detectives to investigate. As the robbers had already fled far away, they returned to the police chief to file the case and secretly arrested them in different locations.

He Boyan Case 174

Kidnappers Receive Heavy Sentences 175

Zhang Aqing and Two Others Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

He Boyan, a steel magnate, was kidnapped at around 11 a.m. on December 27th last year, in front of his residence in Donghua Lane, Xizang Road. He was taken away by kidnappers and hidden in the bandit's den at No. 1 Zhongde Lane, Xiaomuqiao Road, Longhua. A letter was sent demanding a huge ransom. Subsequently, Huatan Inspector Tai Jingfan, detectives Liang Yuliang, Ji Yushan, etc. of the Hui Police Station successively arrested eleven male and female kidnappers, including Zhang Aqing, and rescued the hostage He Boyan. They were sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, the time for sentencing arrived. The police station escorted the defendants to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Special Court. The presiding judge Xue Lanru announced the verdict. The main text stated:

Zhang Aqing, Yang Aqing, and Ji Deming are each sentenced to life imprisonment for kidnapping and extortion, and each is deprived of public rights for life. Lu Asan is sentenced to 15 years of imprisonment for kidnapping and extortion and is deprived of public rights for 15 years. Gu Afu, Lu Yingfan, and Huang Jinlong are each sentenced to 12 years of imprisonment for assisting in kidnapping and extortion, and each is deprived of public rights for 12 years. Zhang Dexing is sentenced to 15 years of imprisonment for assisting in kidnapping and extortion and is deprived of public rights for 15 years. Yang Shankong, Gu Xiaomao, and Gu Daishi are all found not guilty. The guns and ammunition are confiscated. The police lawyer Jiang Baolian requested that the defendants who were found not guilty be remanded in custody during the appeal period. The court approved.

Suzhou Creek

Navigation Was Cut Off Again Yesterday 176

Yesterday afternoon, due to the large number of ships and the falling tide, navigation was cut off again in Suzhou Creek. From Xinda Bridge, Xinzha Bridge, Wuzhen Road Bridge, and Xinlaji Bridge, the ships in the river could be seen packed together like ants. Among them were mainly flour boats, rice straw boats, coal boats, plank boats, brick and tile boats, and steamed bun boats. It was not until nightfall that the situation had not been cleared. At present, the water police are trying to order the ships at both ends to withdraw in order to allow navigation.

Saltwater Rushed into Wusong

The Congee Tasted Bad and Was Hard to Swallow

Opium Addicts Were Busy Hiring Porters

The weather a few days ago was unusually cold. After the heavy snow, it turned sunny and warm, as if it were spring. However, in recent days, the tides have receded, causing saltwater to rush into the mouth of the river. The water in the Wusong area has tasted salty since the day before yesterday, and it was even worse yesterday. The taste was quite salty and bitter. Even the congee cooked in people's homes had a salty taste. All the teahouses experienced sluggish business due to the saltwater. However, beverages are essential for life. This salty tea is not only increasingly thirst-quenching but may also damage the throat. The most deeply feared is its use in cooking opium. Once used mistakenly, it cannot be remedied. Therefore, the usual old opium smokers are busy searching for fresh water. However, the porters from Jiangbei are taking advantage of this opportunity, charging 20 to 30 cents or 40 to 50 cents per load of fresh water. This side business is also quite considerable. It is noted that this saltwater rushes into the mouth of the river every year at the end of the year and the beginning of spring, lasting for two or three days for a short period and six or seven days for a longer period. It occurs once or twice every year. The superstitious villagers call it the New Year's tide, which is the common name for saltwater entering the river.

Shangchuan Bus Adds Ferry Service 181

Operating Between Caojia Road, Gujia Road, Xujia Road, and Huangjiawan

Transportation between Chuansha and Shanghai, with the Shangchuan long-distance bus service, has always been convenient. However, the northern areas, such as Gujia Road, Beicaijia Road, and Huangjiawan, are far from the Puhbin in the west and the bus station in the south. The journey is still long. Usually, transportation relies solely on hand-pushed carts, which are neither economical nor time-saving. Whenever it rains, the roads are slippery and difficult to travel, making the journey even more difficult for travelers. Now, in order to develop transportation convenience for passengers in that area, the company has decided to add a small motorboat from February 1st, operating from Huangjiawan, passing through Xujia Road, Beicaijia Road, Gujia Road, to Caojia Road Station, running back and forth, picking up and dropping off passengers. The one-way boat fare is uniformly eight cents. Passengers who also take the bus will only be charged four cents for the boat fare in addition to the bus ticket. After this line is implemented, passengers in that area will have more convenient transportation, which will surely increase the number of passengers. The departure times are attached below: Huangjiawan departs at 7:00 a.m., 10:00 a.m., 12:30 p.m., and 3:00 p.m. Caojia Road departs at 8:30 a.m., 11:30 a.m., 1:30 p.m., and 4:30 p.m., four trips each. The wharves along the way include Huangjiawan, North Xujia Road South City, (Lukoujiugou), North Caijia Road North City, (Zhaojiagou), Gujia Road, (Hui North School East), Caojia Road (West Side of the Electric Light Factory), etc., five locations.

North China Textile Factory

Sells Products to Raise Funds to Help Women and Children 182

The products of the Tianjin North China Textile Factory cannot be sold in the Northeast due to the impact of Japanese dumping. In addition, cotton yarn prices have plummeted, resulting in cost losses, and accumulated inventory, forming a stranded situation. The factory was originally established during the May 3rd Massacre, when public-spirited people in Shandong Province donated large sums of money to help women and children affected by the disaster. At this time of difficult living conditions, if the factory were to close down and cause further displacement, it would be a cause for concern for social security. Therefore, the factory is selling its products to raise funds in order to reverse the declining trend. Well-known figures in the Shanghai business community received the factory's fundraising appeal yesterday. The original text stated: Since the May 3rd Massacre, compatriots in Shandong Province have risen up to boycott enemy goods and generously donated funds to establish industries. Our factory was established in response to the situation, mainly engaged in dyeing, weaving, and sewing. In the early stages of its establishment, the results were not good, and losses were exhausted. In recent years, we have carefully studied and developed, and our industry has become increasingly advanced. Our products surpass those from abroad in quality, and our scale is fully prepared. Our sales have spread throughout the Northeast provinces. We were expecting to develop, but we have been affected by the Japanese invaders. Our goods cannot be sold in the Northeast provinces, cotton yarn prices have plummeted, resulting in cost losses, and accumulated inventory, forming a stranded situation, making it almost impossible to maintain. However, in recent years, hundreds of women and children affected by disasters have been sent to the factory by public and private organizations to learn industry. They are about to become unemployed and cannot be accommodated. After a public meeting, it was said that at this time of difficult living conditions, society cannot afford to add a large number of unemployed vagrants. Moreover, after several years of operation, the results have been remarkable. Due to the impact of the current situation, the economy is temporarily unable to operate smoothly, resulting in a failure. It is indeed a pity. Rather than closing down and going bankrupt, why not sell products to raise funds? Everyone agreed, so we specially sell products to raise funds, hoping to collect contributions from all sides, and repeatedly ask for introductions in various ways, hoping that Your Excellency's benevolent reputation will spread far and wide, and your high friendship is worthy of admiration. We dare to humbly present several kinds of products, hoping that you will generously donate funds to help us through this difficult time. Not only will our factory be able to maintain our livelihood, but hundreds of poor women and children workers who have no home to return to will not be displaced and will be able to survive, all thanks to the benevolence of Your Excellency. The price of this fundraising is preferably as much as possible, and a small amount is also acceptable. If there are difficulties, you can also return them for other purposes. In recent years, people with lofty ideals have strongly advocated saving the country through industry. You should not be indifferent to our factory's efforts to benefit society and restore our rights. Looking forward to your kind support, we are immensely grateful. We respectfully wish you happiness and attach a list of proposed donation amounts on the left, which can be recognized at will: Support Amount: 100 yuan, Danger Amount: 80 yuan, Stability Amount: 65 yuan, Collapse Amount: 50 yuan.

Shanghai East Tea and Water Industry Agreed on Industry Regulations

Business Will Be Suspended for Half a Day Today

About one hundred and dozens of business owners who operate tea houses and water stoves (commonly known as tiger stoves) in the Yangshupu Lan Road Maohai Road Huade Road area of this city. Recently, due to the high price of coal and large expenses, and the Shanghai Waterworks Company has changed the water contract system (usually the water fee for each household is 6 to 12 yuan per month) to water meter calculation, the monthly water fee has increased to three or four times the amount, which will lead to an inability to maintain the state. A meeting of the industry was convened some days ago to discuss relief measures. As a result, it was agreed to organize the Shanghai East Tea and Water Industry Friendship Association. Shi Dehua, Zhang Zuoxian, Xue Jinzhu, Chen Hongshun, Zhao Jinbiao, Xu De, Xu Mingdong, Huang Dafang, Sheng Kaixian, and other nine people were elected as directors. It was also agreed on industry regulations and other matters. The most important thing is to stop business for half a day starting at 2 pm today (31st). From tomorrow (February 1st), hot water will be uniformly 10 cents for two spoons, each spoon weighing one market catty, in order to avoid unnecessary competition among the industry and maintain business. The water spoon used will be purchased and issued by the association. The overpass next to Tongxing Building on the west end of Taopeng Road, Pingjia Road, was selected as the temporary office. It is also heard that regarding the water fee issue, Attorney Shen Xiaoxiang has been entrusted to ask the waterworks company to maintain the original water contract method.

Hangjiang Road Reduced Freight Rates for Maolu Paper

The Two Roads Still Charge According to the Original Grade

The two roads car department yesterday issued a circular to all stations, saying, "In the case of paper transportation, the method of charging fees according to the three grades of excellent, ordinary, and coarse was notified in the circular No. 2391.12846 on November 14, 22nd year, and ordered to be followed. Now, the Hangjiang Road Transportation Department's letter opened, 'Check the item of Maolu paper, which is a local product of Longyou Yushan on this road. The material is not very good. According to the copy of the letter No. 2391.12846 sent by your office, the fee is charged according to the second-class cargo, which is rather high. Now, in order to promote domestic production and develop industry, it has been approved by the Engineering Bureau to change the fee to the fourth-class cargo. In the future, when the paper is handled for intermodal transport, the freight that should be collected by this road should be checked and collected according to the fourth-class cargo. The corresponding letter should be reached, and please check and order to comply with the letter,' etc., are hereby approved. In the future, at each station, in various paper goods, without the express provisions of the Ministry of Railways, the two roads and the Hangjiang Road intermodal transport will be distinguished, and the Mao deer paper will still be handled according to the original grade in the two roads section. In the case of intermodal transport with the Hangjiang Road, the fee will be charged according to the fourth-class cargo on that road section. It is necessary to follow the order."

Wuhan Invincible Brand Butterfly Cream Counterfeit Case 184

Xu Gongchen Is on the Run with a Reward of 500 Yuan

Accomplice Xu Ruilin Was Sentenced to Two Months in Prison

The Wuhan Zhaijia Lane Huasheng Cosmetic Company, which was opened by the Xu Gongchen and Xu Ruilin brothers, counterfeited the trademark of the Invincible Butterfly Cream of the Home Industry Association last year, intending to confuse the sales of goods. The JingSha Public National Salvation Association discovered the counterfeit goods on November 29 last year and sent a letter to the Shanghai Home Industry Association. The association then sent investigator Zhuang Maoru to Wuhan to report to the Public Security Bureau that various counterfeit trademarks and goods with counterfeit trademarks had been seized at the Huasheng Company. The Public Security Bureau transferred the case to the Hankou District Court for punishment. The case has now been criminally sentenced on January 22, and the main text briefly states: (1) The seized counterfeit Invincible Brand trademarks and various counterfeit trademark goods are confiscated; (2) Xu Ruilin is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for counterfeiting the registered trademark with the intention of deceiving others; (3) Xu Gongchen is on the run and the trial process has been suspended. According to regulations, the association may offer a reward for his arrest. It is heard that the association will offer a reward of 500 yuan within a few days and publish a wanted notice.

The Construction Department of Zhejiang Province has also sent people to survey it. However, the area is originally a coastal area with beautiful scenery, which is an excellent summer resort. It is now heard that representatives of various industries in the area have organized the "Zhapu New Village Construction Association Promotion Association" and have elected preparatory committee members to carry out the work in the near future. The prosperity of the area in the future can be predicted.

Suffering from Mental Illness

Concubine, Overcome by Sadness, Hangs Herself 191

Alimony for Separation Embezzled by Intermediaries

Feeling Desolate, She Chooses Death

Jiang Lanzhen, a woman from Changzhou, is twenty-nine years old this year. She was formerly married as a concubine to Jiao Wenbin from Zhenjiang (currently forty-one years old, residing at No. 33 Hengmao Lane, Baxianqiao, recently suffering from mental illness and unemployed at home). They lived together at No. 13, Dakangfang, Lane 297, Route Cardinal Foch of the French Concession, as the second landlord. She had no children of her own with Jiao, but they adopted four children: the eldest daughter, Yuying, is seventeen years old this year, the second daughter is twelve years old, the youngest daughter is six years old, and the son is eight years old. Recently, due to Jiao's sudden mental illness, the relationship between husband and concubine deteriorated, making it impossible to live in peace. Therefore, around the summer of this year according to the old lunar calendar, through the mediation of mutual friends and relatives, she separated from Jiao, remaining in the original residence. Jiao was to pay her alimony of 1,500 yuan, but most of this amount was consumed by intermediaries, and Jiang actually received only several hundred yuan. Over the past eight or nine months, she had spent almost all of it, and suddenly felt economically distressed. Supporting one son and three daughters, she felt that her life was drifting, without support or reliance, and feeling desolate, she conceived a desperate thought. Therefore, the night before last, while the children and other tenants were sound asleep, at dusk when it was quiet, she took off her trouser belt, hung herself. It was not until eight o'clock yesterday morning that her eldest daughter, Yuying, sleeping upstairs, got up and entered the room, calling for her mother without response, and discovered that she had hanged herself on the side of the bed. She quickly called the neighbors to rescue her, but it was too late. She had already died of suffocation, her body stiff. They immediately notified the French police station, which sent detectives to investigate, and at the same time, the body was transported to the Tongren Fuyuan branch mortuary, waiting for the Second Special District Court to send personnel to examine it today.

Defecating on the Wharf, Falls into the Huangpu River and Drowns 192

Yesterday morning at approximately 9:00 AM, a man, Mr. A, aged approximately fifty, went to the floating bridge of the Taikoo Wharf on the Xinkaihe side of the Bund in the French Concession to defecate. By chance, he was careless and lost his footing, causing him to fall into the river with a splash. He quickly sank to the bottom of the river. The patrolman on the shore saw this and immediately called boatmen to help rescue him ashore, but he was already dead. The patrolman reported to the police station, which sent detectives to investigate. Since there was no address, his surname and given name are unknown, and there is no way to find his family. The body was then transported by car to the Tongren Fuyuan branch mortuary to await examination.

Illegally Selling Narcotic Red Pills, Sentenced 193

Zhang Huisheng, a native of Suzhou, aged twenty-seven, recently illegally sold narcotic red pills for profit in the building at No. 120 Maididian Road, formerly Xinjie, in the French Concession, violating the prohibition order. Detectives Zhou Buguang and Bao Tan Jiyuqing of the French police station learned of this. At 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, they rushed to the address, arrested him, and confiscated a large package and a cloth bag of red pills, totaling 7,300 pills, worth more than one hundred yuan, as well as thirty-five small white cloth bags used to hold the pills. He was taken to the police station and yesterday sent to the Criminal Division One of the Second Special District Court. Acting Judge Qiu Huan-ying took the stand for interrogation. The police lawyer Chen Ming explained the case and prosecuted him according to Article 6 of the Opium Suppression Law, and submitted the evidence. Zhang confessed to the sale without denying it. The court verified the confession and sentenced Zhang Huisheng on the spot for intending to sell and possessing opium substitutes, to eight months of imprisonment and a fine of one hundred yuan, which could be converted into imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention, or two yuan of fine for one day of detention. The red pills were confiscated and burned.

Rickshaw Owner Xu Xiaobo's Home Robbed by Bandits 194

Six or Seven Bandits Injured the Victim's Right Eye

Police Officers Heard the Alarm and Rounded Up, Capturing One Thief on the Spot

A rickshaw owner named Xu Xiaobo, who makes a living by renting out rickshaws, lives at No. 10, Junyi Lane, Dapuqiao Road, Shanghai. Xu, coming from humble origins, knows the hardship of resources, so he is diligent and thrifty. Over the years, he has accumulated some savings, but unexpectedly, he was coveted by bandits. Yesterday morning at approximately 12:10 AM, six or seven bandits suddenly came, speaking with a Jiangbei accent, each holding sharp weapons and pistols. They threatened Xu to keep silent and demanded that he hand over money and valuables. Xu resisted slightly, and one bandit immediately injured Xu's right eye and kept watch over him. The other five bandits then scattered to plunder, which lasted about half an hour, before each carrying their loot and fleeing. After the incident, a detailed investigation of the losses revealed that in addition to cash, silver dollars, and copper coins totaling about one hundred yuan, along with gold jewelry and clothing, the total was about two hundred and fifty yuan. Unexpectedly, at this critical moment, the Second District United Office had already received the news. The patrol officer Zhang Fude of the Rihuiqiao substation led a large number of police officers to round up from all sides, chasing directly to the intersection of Xietu Road and Dapu Road, intercepting one thief, seizing a six-inch pistol with the serial number 96883, and nine bullets, and taking him to the district for strict interrogation. According to the confession, his name is Xu Laoer, thirty-four years old, from Zhenjiang, living on a boat in Caojiadu. He had accomplices Wang Jinshan and Zhou Jinbao, and had invited three strangers to conspire to rob. After the confession, District Chief Li immediately prepared a document to submit to the Third Section for interrogation, and at the same time ordered his subordinates to strictly arrest the accomplices and bring them to justice.

Two Celebrities Come to Shanghai Together 195

Go master Gu Shui-ru and calligrapher Ren Cixiang have recently returned from the north and are staying at the residence of the owner of Yin Lu. Yesterday, a banquet was specially held to welcome the two gentlemen. More than ten people including the famous doctor Tao Muzhang were present. Mr. Gu's chess skills have long been famous at home and abroad. Mr. Ren has been studying calligraphy for many years. During the banquet, the owner asked for calligraphy to keep as a souvenir. Mr. Ren generously wrote a couplet saying (Moving strange rocks to deceive thin monks, not crushing flower bushes for many guests). His writing is like holding an egg, and his movement of the brush is like a hanging needle. When the tip of the brush touches the paper, where it is moist, ink lines rise, and where it is dry, thousands of hairs exert force together. His structure is like seal script entering running script, and also like eight parts entering cursive script, simple and vigorous, truly the style of the Qin and Han dynasties. All the gentlemen present added their praises, believing that since the passing of Gao Yongzhi, Wu Changshuo, Qing Daoren, Zeng Nongran and other artists in Shanghai, the art world has long felt desolate. Today, Ren Zi has stopped in Shanghai and is happy to form a calligraphy connection with scholars who know calligraphy on the sea. Those who want to obtain Mr. Ren's calligraphy treasures can ask Chen Changyi of Jiangzhe Bank and Cai Shenfu of the Shen Bao Editorial Department for the price list.

Police Officer Opens Fire and Captures Bandit Alive 196

Rencheng Ning Style Loan Instrument Shop, opened at No. 5 Xihuali, intersection of Dongxi Huade Road and Gongping Road. They then threatened the owner to hand over the keys to the safe and recklessly searched. After about half an hour, they left with their loot, which included more than eighty yuan in cash and jewelry. However, the victim also tracked them out, and the bandits did not notice. When they walked out of the lane entrance, the four bandits fled in different directions. One of the bandits fled towards Gongping Road. At that time, the victim was afraid that they would all escape, so he also chased closely towards Gongping Road. There happened to be a Chinese police officer on duty there, and the victim immediately reported to the officer. The officer rushed forward to pursue him and ordered him to stop. Unexpectedly, the bandit ran wildly all the way, so the officer drew his gun and fired a shot at the bandit's right leg. The bandit immediately fell to the ground and was captured. A pistol, several bullets, and stolen goods such as diamond rings were found on his person, and he was taken to the police station together. Detectives were sent out to hunt down accomplices, and the wounded bandit was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. After he recovers, he will be interrogated.

Reading Q&A

The Fundamental Problems of Reading (Part 3) 207

(3) The Path of Self-Study

Yesterday I spoke from the perspective of the purpose of reading, and now I will talk about the methods of reading.

The method of reading is the steps that a beginner should take. We now divide it into five stages. Most of our readers are dropouts, and their foundation in writing is not very solid. Therefore, we believe that the first step in reading is to make the reader's tool, that is, writing, fluent. We know that reading must be able to understand the words; if you can't understand the words in the book, how can you understand the content of the book? But now, many readers are making this mistake. They often write many bad comments on the books they return to our library, saying how obscure the writing is, or how stiff the translation is. Of course, many books are indeed like this, but after we have carefully read many books (because of the readers' suggestions), we feel that the writing is not very bad or difficult to understand, and these books are mostly literary books, without specialized terms and the need for considerable knowledge to understand. Therefore, we have to say that this is because the reader's writing skills are not enough and the reading is not serious. Therefore, we hope that readers with weak literary foundations will pay more attention to this, because this is a prerequisite for reading. However, learning to write, except for those who want to study linguistics, is just a tool. It is enough for us to learn to understand modern Chinese and write clear articles. However, we should not spend a lot of time on writing, because our country's science is backward, and many people advocate that readers must read foreign languages. We cannot fully agree with this point. The reasons have been seen in several questions about choosing subjects (see this column on January 13th and 14th). Readers should be able to review and will not repeat them.

The above is the first stage of reading. The work in this stage can be carried out simultaneously with the preparation stage mentioned above, or completed before. After the above two steps are completed, the choice of subjects has been decided, and the tools for reading can also be said to be in order, so you can start to study the subject you have chosen. At the beginning, we advocate reading a book of this subject "Introduction" "Outline" and the like, must be the contents of the subject, the basic concepts in mind. At this stage, reading is not about "more", but about "precision". Because in the early stages of learning, the most feared thing is not being able to get a systematic concept, but being filled with a stomach of fragmented and chaotic knowledge. Therefore, "intensive reading" (Intensive Work) is the only principle that beginners must follow. When the editor was reading in the early years of university, because of his high desire for knowledge, he liked to read many books quickly, but as a result, not only did his knowledge not become richer, but it also made the basic concepts of the subjects he studied unclear. This is the painful experience of the editor. Now it is too late to regret it, and I hope that those who are determined to read will not repeat my "mistakes". If the reader already has a rough understanding of the basic knowledge, then the next reading work is not to read many specialized works, not to study various theories, not to study the development history of the subject, not to do research on certain small problems... but to study "the methodology of learning". Now, because the whole society is in an era of great upheaval, various theories are emerging. We are seeking the truth in these chaotic theories. It is really not an easy task, but it is also not a difficult task. Because the differences in theories are mostly due to the different points of view and "the different methodologies adopted". If we can lay a solid foundation for "the methodology of learning", I think there will be no such thing as being "entangled by various theories". Therefore, we believe that the central work of the third stage is best to study the methodology of learning. However, it is not possible to have only methods and no materials, so the work of the fourth stage of reading is "extensive reading" (Extensive Work). The so-called "extensive reading" is to broaden your knowledge and expand your scope of knowledge. Because once the scope of knowledge is wide, you will not fall into "ignorance" and will not be blinded by a certain theory. (Readers can refer to this column on January 10th, "The Divergence of Theories and the Grasp of Correct Theories"). In this stage of "extensive reading". At the same time, readers should also extend to many subjects that are related to the subject they are studying. For example, those who study "Economics" should not only have read many famous economic works, specialized economic problems, and books on economic history, but also need to study other subjects, such as psychology, statistics, and political science. Because the entire activity of human beings cannot be divided into economic, political... but in science, for the convenience of research, it can be divided into many categories of subject names. Moreover, there are many tool subjects for academic research, such as writing and statistics. Therefore, in order to make the subjects we study profound, other auxiliary and related subjects must be read as well. The self-study process has been described in general. However, there are several points to pay attention to when self-studying according to this process, which are mentioned here by the way: (1) The selection of books must be strict, because reading books that distort the facts is worse than not reading books. This condition should be paid special attention to when doing "preparation" and "intensive reading" work. (2) Reading books should be economical. There are really many books now, and it is impossible for one person to read all the books. However, readers should not be angry, because there are many books that are really unnecessary to read. Therefore, when reading a certain book, readers must consider whether reading it is more beneficial than reading other books, and whether it is economical in terms of time and energy. (3) When "extensively reading" and "studying other auxiliary subjects", you should compare their importance, and you should think in your heart: Is "extensive reading" more important, or is "studying other auxiliary subjects" more important?

(4) Do not hinder the "purposeful learning" for the sake of learning "means". For example, if learning "statistics" is for the sake of studying "economics", then you must not spend endless time learning "statistics" and put "economics" aside. There are more than a few points that should be paid attention to in self-study, and even these few points still need to be discussed in detail. However, this letter has been written very long, so the unfinished words have to be left for discussion when necessary in the future, ｜Kang｜
