Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

On the Rent Reduction Movement 281

— Li Zhai

Anyone with a little experience living in Shanghai will surely feel that the rent problem is the heaviest burden of their entire life. Workers who toil every day to earn thirty to fifty cents, even though they live in filthy and cramped slums like pigeon cages, still have to spend two dollars a month for half a bed space, or three dollars for half an attic or a small room. A white-collar worker with a monthly income of about fifty dollars finds it hard to keep his rent below ten dollars, while a freelancer with an income of about a hundred dollars spends around thirty dollars on rent. Rent expenses account for more than a quarter of the total income of these people. Therefore, they not only have to shed extra blood and sweat for the landlords, but also constantly toss and turn in agony over the rent problem. As for important figures who have fallen from political grace or wealthy merchants with a knack for making money, some buy their own houses, while others spend eighty to a hundred taels a month on rent, which is like plucking a hair from a bull. The rent problem is of no concern to these "people above people."

Because rental income is a high-interest and very stable source of income, all capitalists, bureaucrats, and various resident foreigners in Shanghai focus their attention on the real estate business through their money-grubbing ways. Amid the current social situation of economic depression in all sectors, this has created a distorted phenomenon where investment in the real estate business is the most active, enjoying unique prosperity. Landlords or major landlords exploit the second landlords using "scientific methods," while the second landlords exploit the third tenants using "Shanghai tricks." In between, there is a group of "reaching generals" of rent-collecting clerks who come up with all kinds of tricks like "extra rent," "hidden fees," and "key money" to extract money from Shanghai residents. The rent-collecting clerks display the same arrogance as collecting police donations to intimidate the second landlords, and the second landlords put on a most unhygienic face to deal with the third tenants. As a result, the general public becomes thinner and thinner, while the major landlords become fatter and fatter. The income of the intermediary layers and the second landlords is also considerable.

Because the "housing" problem in Shanghai is the most distorted and the "tricks" are the most complicated, it is very difficult to rent either newly built houses with sanitary facilities or older houses with lower rents. Renting newly built houses is almost always calculated in taels of silver, at least thirty-five taels or more. With one month's rent as deposit, one month's rent in advance, and renovation costs, one cannot even inquire without two or three hundred dollars. In the case of older houses with slightly lower rents that will not be renovated recently, there is definitely a layer of heavy exploitation by the original tenants. The so-called "renovation," which consists of nothing more than a few electric lights, is said to require a "transfer fee" of five hundred to eight hundred dollars. For city houses located in the commercial center, extra rent easily reaches thousands of dollars, and hidden fees often amount to tens of thousands. Since the rent is expensive and the rules are numerous, the property tax is also incredibly high. The annual extra tax for the Yile Garden on Nanjing Road has increased to 7,500 dollars this year, and that for Tong Huaichun has increased to 6,240 dollars. With these property tax figures that can be viewed as a world wonder, we truly cannot help but admit that they are both "great" and "big"! "The wool comes from the sheep." Those who pay high prices for hidden fees, transfer fees, extra rent, property tax, and rent have no reason to pay out of their own pockets. As a result, they naturally pass on all the losses to the common people of Shanghai. Isn't it the small citizens and the working masses who suffer?

The soaring rent and land prices in Shanghai year after year are certainly not entirely due to the manipulation of capitalists, but also to other reasons. One is that domestic warfare and bankruptcy have made the trend of the rich and the poor concentrating in cities even more acute. The former indirectly increased the source of investment in the real estate industry, and the latter increased the demand for housing in Shanghai society. The second is that in recent years, the number of great figures who have scraped the land with a bold spirit and filled their own pockets has increased compared to the past. The most "safe" areas in their minds, besides the United States, Switzerland, Hong Kong, and Dalian, are the "British Concession" or "French Concession" in Shanghai. They not only build private residences for their own enjoyment, but also build many new lane houses and villages to "serve society"!

When things reach an extreme, they will revert. The burden of rent is oppressing the vast majority of Shanghai citizens to the point of difficulty in breathing. Therefore, the recent rent reduction movement has developed from a widespread sentiment into a broad action. The declaration of various Shanghai organizations to reduce rent says: "If one cannot live in peace and work with joy, it is not just the inability of one family or one store to survive, but the common inability of all families and stores in the city to survive. Moreover, those who come from poor areas and obtain the qualification of Shanghai tenants are even more unable to survive." This is not simply complaining, but a tragic cry of blood and tears mixed together from the citizens of Shanghai!

A Maiden Before Marriage 282

— Cheng Zhang

I don't know why, even I can't figure it out! Lately, my heart always feels a kind of indescribable sweetness!

Sometimes, they nag that I'm acting like a new bride. Staying with him all day long, and no longer playing with them! But then, a surge of heat rushes to my ears, and I get annoyed! They tease me mischievously, saying: Your face is so red, like a big persimmon cake! Really, I feel shy and excited! I think of him, a lovely shadow! My Chen ge! I can't help but smile to myself, but then I pull back as if someone is watching!

Mom is the busiest because of my marriage! And the most painstaking. She always thinks of the trivial things that I don't even think of. She asks the same questions over and over again, sometimes it really makes me annoyed! But later, when I think about it carefully, only my mother truly loves and cares for me wholeheartedly. Item by item, preparing the dowry is the most worrying!

I often tell Mom that we don't need too much! After all, we can still add to it later. But now, after preparing so much all at once, it won't be suitable after a while. Throwing it away wouldn't be worth it! We just need a fully sweet and happy family organization. Chen ge said. So, you'll never change your heart? I probe, also feeling uneasy! I only love you. Chen ge looks at your face, and he feels happy! I don't know what it means to change your heart?

Truly, he is all heart! Just like me, he is honest and doesn't lie. And he keeps his whole sincere heart! Naturally, he is a child! A child would never lie in front of his beloved. I like him, and I love him even more! Occasionally, we meet. We talk about the decoration and furnishings of the home and the furniture to be used in the rooms. He advocates using cream-colored wooden furniture. But I prefer everything to be painted white! Clean and beautiful.

The result of the discussion is that he wins, the reason being: White is too monotonous; cream color doesn't feel monotonous in its cleanliness and is still so beautiful and good-looking! That's how he smiles! Because he has won! Otherwise, he pouts his lips, which is so cute! Like a naughty child who can't get his favorite candy and is equally dissatisfied!

I said, our income and expenditure must have a fixed budget; we can't spend beyond our income! In particular, we should set aside a considerable portion to prepare for our children's education fund. In addition, we also need appropriate entertainment to relieve the fatigue of everyday life! Appropriately, every week in the morning, strolling through the park, the quiet scenery will influence a good mood! In the afternoon, we should enjoy ourselves as much as possible, watching movies, or staying at home, singing songs, and listening to songs, which are all the best forms of entertainment!

Chen ge promised me. To buy a large piano and a wireless radio. I happily hugged his face and kissed him! He laughed. Saying that I am an innocent child, even more lovable than his own younger sister.

Later, I said that I wanted to learn to play the harmonica. It's a great instrument, and I must learn it! Ah, but he wouldn't allow it! Because with my not-so-strong body, it's easy to damage the rapidly expanding part of my lungs!

So, I didn't play the harmonica, and I only played the piano every day. Sometimes, my fingers swelled up and felt numb! But I still couldn't change that excited habit.

But these days, I haven't been playing as often. I'm busy with another reason, of course I know it myself, and others can guess it! Yesterday, Sister Hui asked me. Why I wasn't in the mood to play the piano anymore! Could it be that Chen ge wouldn't let me play it because my hands were so swollen! But! Feeling embarrassed to answer, I just gave her a red face! The days are getting closer and closer, and my heart is beating even harder. Happy anticipation? Shy coquettishness? I can't describe it anymore!

On Unemployed Intellectuals 283

— Wen

Every spring and autumn when schools start, I often see advertisements in the classifieds for teachers, with salaries of two hundred dollars offered for foreign-returned professors, of course, there are some, but advertisements for elementary or middle school teachers with "half-paid volunteer" positions and "own board and lodging" for a measly ten or fifteen dollars for "transportation fees" are everywhere. Also, according to friends I know, there are even some who teach arithmetic and English for twenty dollars a month, teaching more than fourteen hours a week. In addition, the salaries of teachers in many private middle schools are mostly fifty or seventy cents per hour, at most one dollar. If a "boss" starts a middle school and hires teachers for one dollar and twenty cents per hour, many intellectuals on the brink of starvation simply "worry only about not being able to snatch the opportunity"! I also saw an introduction to "maids seeking employment" in the Women's Voice bi-monthly, where "Aunt Chen" was asking for a monthly wage of seven or eight dollars.

The most prevalent and cruel facts above, at least show that the panic of the "unemployed intellectuals" has reached its peak, and many are seeking "special bargains" but cannot find employers; secondly, there are a group of "enthusiastic education" private school bosses who take the exploitation of the brains and sweat of poor teachers as their "lifestyle"; thirdly, the salaries for teachers in many small schools are no better than hiring an old nanny in a second or third-class mansion.

The large number of unemployed intellectuals filling society is naturally the inevitable result of social depression and universal bankruptcy. Under the modality of the era, where there is no order, even though there is "One person becomes Buddha, even his pets ascend to heaven," there is a general depression from the city to the village,

Page 19

the tide pushes the original intellectuals out of the gates of institutions, schools, shops, and companies. And for those "new intellectuals" with university or high school diplomas to get a foothold is obviously impossible.

The accumulation of old and new unemployed intellectuals has almost formed a "mountain of people" shoulder to shoulder, this mountain decorates the major cities, becoming an alarming social tumor. Where are these many unemployed intellectuals going? Naturally, there are only two roads: progress and regression. They cannot linger on the crossroads forever, and there is no "middle way" that is neither biased nor deviated.

Those who are willing to move forward should grasp the true trends of the world and China, and find a way out of the struggle for national independence and the welfare of the people. In terms of personal life, in addition to finding ways to solve the employment problem, they must also strive to politicize their lives. Those who are willing to regress, the problem is even simpler. Take off the "noble" coat, and honestly be a henchman of the old social forces. Even if one cannot become famous, at least one will be a specimen in the dog's pedigree for thousands of years. In short, unemployed intellectuals should not continue to be pessimistic and sigh, nor should they linger in the middle. They should strive for employment on the one hand, and recognize where they are going in the future. Standing on the stage of the war of dragons and tigers and fantasizing about neutrality is the stupidest thing to do and is bound to be "attacked from both sides"!

A Blind Talk on the Guide to Seeking Officialdom 284

— Dao

One day a guest came and described the poor and ugly state of the "disaster officials" waiting for work in Nanjing, which made everyone laugh. However, one couldn't help but sigh and say, "The ups and downs of officialdom have existed since ancient times, but I didn't expect them to be even more severe today!" The guest said, "Do you know how many disaster officials are waiting for work in Nanjing? More than eighteen thousand! Some live in small hotels, some live in the homes of friends and relatives. Only God knows how poor and painful their lives are! However, no matter how poor their lives are, they still have to pay attention to their clothes. Those who wear Zhongshan suits or military uniforms are still the same, but those who wear long robes must have a mandarin jacket, and those who wear Western suits must have an overcoat. Clothes are the appearance of a person, and they must pay attention to them. Moreover, this society only values clothes and not people, isn't that right? They ask friends and relatives to write letters of recommendation every day, and they take the letters of recommendation to see the people they want to see, begging for cultivation and promotion with humble and respectful attitudes. But what is the result, do you know? The important people in Nanjing treat the words 'request for cultivation and promotion' like the wind in their ears, blowing in from the left ear and running out from the right ear, not paying any attention to them at all. Moreover, they are tired of hearing them. Who would want to find a place for this group of disaster officials to eat? As a result, the person you ask for cultivation and promotion gives you a letter of recommendation and asks you to find someone else to cultivate and promote you. You get a letter of recommendation from such an important person, thinking that with his recommendation, the job will definitely be no problem, but that is a piece of waste paper and has no effect at all. Hahaha, you take this important person's letter of recommendation to find that important person for 'cultivation and promotion', and that important person is also a person who is used to issuing letters of recommendation asking people to find another important person for 'cultivation and promotion'. In this way, your letter of recommendation is just a joke to him. "Could it be that this important person's face has completely lost its effect on that important person and they both know it tacitly?" Someone in the audience asked suspiciously. The guest said, "That's right. They are all people who are used to issuing letters of recommendation. When they meet, they don't even bother to mention it. Who ever thought that it was a matter of losing their own face? Poor these eighteen thousand disaster officials, they are still kept in the dark. As soon as the letter of recommendation is sent, their hearts are filled with hope and they happily wait for news at home for ten days or so. After you visit three or two times to inquire, at first you only hear some perfunctory words, and later they even refuse to see you. The doorman often sees you, a disaster official who brings a letter of recommendation to visit his master, and the kind of contemptuous face he gives you is unbearable. You, who have been ordered by the master to refuse to meet you, are like a beggar begging for food from his doorman at that time, and there is no place to complain about the humiliation." "Then, is it impossible to seek employment in Nanjing?" Someone in the audience asked again. The guest said, "That's not entirely true. First, you must have capital, and second, you must put on airs." "Seeking employment also requires capital, then why would people with capital seek employment?" The guest said, "So you are an amateur. Having capital is very useful. Sending gifts requires money, this is one point. Secondly, using money to treat guests to a big meal is the only way to build a relationship. Once you have a relationship, it will be easy to handle. For those who ask for things to be done, after sending gifts and treating them to a meal, your impression will be in his mind, and it will not be difficult to find a job later. However, you must not mention the words 'cultivation and promotion' when sending gifts and treating them to a meal, otherwise it will be over, and he will hate you." "Is this what you call putting on airs?" The guest said, "This is a way to approach him, it is not putting on airs yet. What is meant by putting on airs is that when you meet, you must absolutely put on an expression and attitude of just coming to Nanjing to have fun, so that he has no doubts. And at the same time, you must also show that you don't care about finding a job, that is, you have contact with all parties in the world, and you don't want to find a job. This is putting on airs. Moreover, you must also be able to brag, with a thorough understanding of international situations, domestic politics, Mussolini, Hitler, and even the knowledge of ancient poetry, Song lyrics, novels, and dramas, bragging for a long time and making people admire your erudition, this is enough qualification." "What are the next steps after these steps are done?" The guest said, "Then you proceed to find a job. But you must never mention it in person, it will also be ruined if you mention it yourself, you must entrust a friend to praise you to the skies by his side, let him say it, and it will be done." The guest's words can truly be used as a guide to seeking officialdom. However, the way to seek officialdom is also difficult!

"Year" and "Week" 285

— Wei Ba

Recently, it seems very difficult to live life. One must come up with many methods and set many topics in order to pass the days. This situation did not exist in the past. Outwardly, there were also times in the past when the reign title was changed, or the reign title was named "He Ping," or the reign title was named "Jia He," similar to the current "National Goods Year," "Children's Year," etc., but in essence, they were quite different.

In the past, it was not that the reign title of "He Ping" was set first, and then steps were taken to achieve peace, or that the topic of "Jia He" was proposed, and then steps were taken to produce rice with two, three, or even five or six ears, but rather "a celebration after the fact"! But recently, this is not possible. Recently, it is like writing an essay, where the topic is set first, and then the year is lived.

Although "another year easily passes with autumn wind," the days still pass the same - the suffering still suffer, and the rampant still run rampant. However, the general public needs stimulation. It is necessary to add "what year" or "what week" to ordinary days in order to create temporary excitement. This shows that people's hearts have become unusually tired and can no longer tolerate an ordinary life. However, pursuing what one hopes for in this way is also a wrong path, and one will fall into greater fatigue and a more boring situation, and there will never be a day of "getting what one wants." Russell once said, "Stimulating things, like drugs, the more you have, the more you need." We only need to look at last year's so-called "National Goods Year," and the total import surplus for the whole year reached more than 41.784 million yuan to know. How do people generally feel about "years" or "weeks" that are prepared with great enthusiasm? People's hearts have long since moved from "fatigue" to "numbness," and cannot be stirred up by general slogans - whether stimulation can be effective also has its objective conditions, and the stimulation method we are currently using is like smoking opium, hoping to be excited for a while, or anesthetized for a while!

Novel

A Lonely Person 286

— Dai Ni

Ke Jia seemed to sense that Bai E's behavior was unusual. He moved his gaze to the desk, where a can of cigarettes was placed neatly. "Brother, are you smoking again?" It wasn't intentionally meant to be the beginning of loneliness. An uncultivated athlete cannot reveal his emotions with facial expressions. What he knows is being honest and impolite, especially towards Zhu Xiaosun, whom he calls his little brother. He believes that his orders should be questioned unless they are revoked. "Smoking? I can even drink!" The corners of his mouth twitched nervously, coldly like a hidden weapon. Ke Jia smiled, unnaturally. "Brother, did you see my note?" He rubbed his hands together, as if hoping to elicit the answer from the other person with this gesture.

He nodded, not answering. "Where exactly did you stay for two days?" He leaned forward, as if preparing for the 50-meter final race with his hands close to the floor. "On the mountain!" "The doctor said so." "It was my own idea!" He took the last puff of smoke so elegantly, throwing the cigarette butt out the window with a practiced technique. Then the hand that pulled back extracted two cigarettes from the cigarette can, gave one to Ke Jia, and said with a slight smile, "Let's smoke cigarettes." This was equivalent to the honesty and impoliteness of a wild bull. Telling you that you can smoke here, but you can't talk. The white smoke drifted out the window with the gentle breeze, lightly. A long period of silence occupied the space of March.

Like a rejected athlete on the playing field, Ke Jia stood up and said, "You're definitely not going to Shanghai?" "Why wouldn't I go to Shanghai?" A smile. A frown. "After your wedding, I will go to Shanghai myself." "What does that mean?" He said, unconsciously sitting down. "Am I going to ask you again if being lovelorn is painful?" He smiled beautifully. But then he tightened his face. "I don't want to see Qin Bo again." The wild bull, who had been guessing the riddle for a long time, finally couldn't help but laugh. "Brother, don't be childish. The day before yesterday, Jing Yi..." Ke thought for a moment, and then continued, "It was the day before yesterday that she visited Qin Bo and asked her to be the bridesmaid. She immediately agreed. She also asked if you could come back from Hangzhou. Brother, love is just a game to embellish life. If Qin Bo marries, you can play another one. Is a man's capacity really so narrow?" He spoke every word with great force, showing that he was an athlete. Xiaosun brushed his naturally curly hair and suddenly jumped up from the desk chair. A white goose swimming leisurely in a clear stream, he did not admit that his capacity was inferior to that of a woman. "Enough talk! When are you leaving?" "Tomorrow." "Let's go together!" His naturally curly hair swayed in the spring breeze of March.

Film Weekly

"The Storm Over Mexico" Director Eisenstein's Autobiography (Part 2) 287

— Translated by Shu Yin

1922 was a crucial year!

My connection with the revolution became a kind of inner confidence, of blood and bone. In my creative process, I transitioned from the rational, almost abstract, and eccentric "The Sage" (adapted from Ostrovsky's comedy) to the propagandistic and inflammatory street dramas "Hear Moscow" and "Gas Masks," and finally to the revolutionary film "Potemkin."

The tendency to gradually approach the revolution made art more deeply imbued with the elements of militant materialism.

Continuing to make films and meet the demands of society, I continued to take on the task of developing a "method" to create cinematic expressions, striving to instill effective revolutionary art and arm the young people engaged in film work during the first Five-Year Plan. Recent central works like "Ten Days That Shook the World" were intended for experimentation and research.

My personal work currently takes completely consistent steps with the scientific and educational experimental methods planned by the State Institute of Cinematography. Theoretical writings are based on the fundamental principles of film art. I have created my life philosophy, which is entirely based on the interests of the revolution, because the revolution determines everything.

The question here is to what extent the development of consciousness can reach, and the will is unyielding. When I reached such a stage, I decided to travel abroad. Abroad—is a final test for the biography of a citizen who grew up in the Soviet society of the October Revolution. This is a test of free choice. Abroad—is a final test for the "masters of culture" to consciously distinguish friends from enemies. Abroad—is a final test for creators to know whether they can create revolution alone and survive outside the revolution. This test took place in front of the gold mine of Hollywood. The means of wanting to reject human charm and grace with a non-heroic posture were rejected. They were working for the benefit of another class under different social circumstances. It is impossible to create outside this class division. The full power and ability of the revolution has risen. The pressure of the proletarian revolution sweeps away all resistance in its path and pulls in forces that once tended towards it, grasping them even more strongly. That is what every Soviet artist does and thinks. Many of us come from the revolution. All of us participate in the revolution with the weapons of art. (The End)

Film Review

Review of "Cradle Song" 288

— Ling He

Cradle Song

Paramount Pictures · Grand Theater Premiere

(1)

Since "The Woman" shook the film industry, in addition to the ideological system of the director, Ms. Stone, radiating a rare brilliance in the European and American film circles, the protagonist, Dolores del Río, also received deep attention and was immediately hired by Paramount from Germany to America.

(2)

Now, after watching this film, we cannot help but immediately recall "The Woman." This is not only due to the relationship of the leading actor, but also the arrangement of the story is quite similar. "The Woman," as everyone knows, declares the freedom of human nature. For freedom, for love between people, those "uniformed virgins" are unwilling to endure suffering and instinctively resist oppressors. Their spirit of fighting for freedom and justice has undoubtedly given some degree of stimulation to those who are uneasy with reality.

So, what does "Cradle Song" tell us? Religion, the ruler of the spirit, has ruined the youth of countless young girls. They are anesthetized in that illusory so-called "universal love" of holy light, and from the desolate world, they move towards the hell of heaven. There, although they have been baptized by God, they still cannot forget the people outside the convent, their homes, their siblings, and all the people who care about them. Although they try their best to endure the cold and cruel trampling and destruction of God, they also cannot forget the existence of love between people. Therefore, they issued a weak call for liberation from the depths of their hearts, and thus Teeresa, who was raised by Joana, finally escaped from that cold convent in the exchange of their sorrows and joys. The profound depiction of human feelings, the mournful cry of the weak religious prisoners. Obviously, this does not have the passion of "The Woman," but the tone is very similar to "The Woman." The former is active, while the latter is the opposite. This further proves the greatness of Ms. Stone.

(3)

In addition, what should be especially mentioned is the attitude of the author of "Cradle Song." On the one hand, he has an irrational expression against religion, but he never attacks the existence of monasteries. He completely uses his doctrine of the mean to promote the common sense of human feelings. As for letting the female lead leave the convent and then the scope of being a good wife and loving mother, that is certainly something we are overly demanding that he cannot understand. Therefore, in American movies, it is already worth paying attention to having such a rational work. As for this film, it is entirely for Dolores del Río's personality and style, which is extremely obvious.

(4)

"The Broadway Melody" 289

For years, the most outstanding song and dance film is the Lianhua production. The scenery is novel, the scale is grand, and talented people gather. Over fifty Broadway stars are recruited to participate. The songs and dances and the plot are both superb. It will be premiered in Nanjing soon.

This film is always a good work. Not only is the story as mentioned above, but the director's technique is also worth praising. But here, I don't want to point out every single detail. What must be said is its main feature.

After watching it, stories of this type are often easy to become boring, but here, emotions are moved in a quiet atmosphere. Whether it is the effect of sound, or the melody of the play, or even the composition of each written surface, they are extremely perfect. In terms of art itself, it once again confirms the great true value of film. The acting is good, and this should be praised by everyone. I don't want to comment on the skills of each actor here, anyway, they have all tried their best to achieve extremely high results. However, Dolores del Río seems to be developing only within this typical personality, and it always feels somewhat narrow.

After Seeing "Cradle Song" 290

— Shen Bai

(1) Spring in Winter

After "January 28th", in such cold winter weather, coupled with my own chaotic emotions, I feel extremely cold... "Cradle Song" gave me some kind air. It can also be said to be a momentary spring in winter... (2) There is no golden feature here.

Eroticism, wild dancing, women's legs, "mmm..." These are the characteristics of general American films, which is like the afterglow of the setting sun, a general beauty. But there is nothing in this film, there is only the tears of human feelings...

(3) A Few Points Worth Remembering.

That same-tone Follow Shot; the melody that connects the scenes between the screens with music; the pyramid-shaped "Bust" composition that represents sublimity; the combination of these made the depths of my eyes feel slightly moist. Note one a, on the cold and lonely picture of Joana kneeling in front of the Virgin Mary statue, the music is the tone of an external Spanish hot dance. b· When Joana is standing alone by the wall, the music is the cheers of children outside... These inverse comparisons of sound and picture are worth remembering. Note 2: All of Joana's half-length shots use pyramid-shaped compositions.

"Fiery Youth" Premieres at the Carlton 291

The Tianyi Film Company recently produced "Fiery Youth," directed by Tang Jie, starring Wang Yuanlong and Ye Qiuxin, with Zhang Zhenduo, Ma Dongwu, Xiao Zhengzhong, Shao Gang, and others in supporting roles. Wang Yuanlong has always been known as the Silver Screen Overlord, and Ye Qiuxin is a rising star, praised as a model of beauty. The two collaborated for the first time, and the results were very satisfactory. The film depicts the despicable tricks of unscrupulous merchants and the spirit of patriotic youth who are not threatened by coercion or enticed by profit. The whole play is enthusiastic and intense, enough to arouse the sympathy of the audience. It has been decided that the film will be publicly screened at the Carlton Grand Theatre starting on January 31.

Novel Film Fiery Youth (Part 2) 292

— Long Geng

"Dad! I have some too!" The son in the corner shouted. He had a piggy bank full of money. That's how their cloth shop opened! The shop's name was "Xie Xing." Kejian's father was the manager, Kejian greeted customers at the shop, Kejian's mother wrapped the cloth, Kejian's wife and sister turned the cloth over for the customers to see, and the little son Shixiong passed the cloth and invoices. This family store was too enviable! The Xie Xing cloth shop was full of vitality, and many customers patronized it one after another. However, unfortunately, this thriving Xie Xing was seen by that cunning monkey-like Diaoren. He was jealous, and he even remembered the past. Therefore, he wanted to give Kejian a serious revenge. Immediately, Diaoren hurriedly ran back and reported everything to Hao Xin. After considerable consideration by the two of them, their method emerged. They opened a Da Xing cloth shop directly across from Xie Xing. The entrance of Da Xing was surrounded by large red and purple colorful cloths, and Connaught also played loudly at the entrance. The large golden characters at the entrance told people that they were having a 30% off sale. Under the banner of this 30% off sale, crowds of customers surged like a tide, bustling. But, what about Xie Xing on the other side? Kejian's father and son were surrounded by a melancholy atmosphere. They glared angrily at the lively and prosperous scene across the street, and were silently stunned. "Selling at 30% off will lose 15% of the cost, how can we do it? But if we don't, we won't even have money to eat, what can we do? We can only temporarily follow them." So, Xie Xing also sold at 30% off. But Da Xing sold even cheaper at 50% off. Kejian's father was extremely embarrassed, and Kejian could only sigh a long sigh. But, at the same time, debt collectors were roaring in their store, so Kejian's father's heart was broken. Under multiple squeezes, Kejian's father fell ill. At the same time, a transfer advertisement was posted at the entrance of Xie Xing. Diaoren saw the transfer advertisement and showed a victorious smile. He walked into the store and asked Kejian: "Is the store really going to be transferred?" Kejian was lost in thought, revealing a mysterious expression of dissatisfaction. "How much is the stock worth?" On the one hand, he still asked with a treacherous smile. But, on the one hand, he still ignored him. "How much do you want for the transfer?" Diaoren asked again. "Including everything, just 1,000 yuan is fine." Kejian said with an angry tone. So, Diaoren retreated with a treacherous smile. But, Kejian's wife next to him couldn't bear it anymore. She said: "It's rare for someone to come and inquire, but you ask for such a high price that you scare people away all at once." Kejian said angrily, "If they run, they run. I originally didn't want to transfer it to him." "He, people don't get along with you, but money has no grudge against you! Don't you know that the family urgently needs money?" (To be continued)
